# Introduction | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

![Page cover](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FioaW93P1MscfVyNlUTh4%252F0.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb385b6a-1714-4803-a56d-fccde133f780&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=275a82ce&sv=2)

Welcome to the Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.10 Service Pack 1 Essentials course. This course provides an overview of the **Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator (ePO) - On-prem product**, key features, purpose, and benefits. You will also learn how to install, configure, operate, and troubleshoot issues relating to ePO.

The Course is divided into lessons and a final exam.

Each lesson is a combination of instructional material such as texts, videos, external links, knowledge checks, and interactive learning experiences.

To successfully complete this training, you need to take and pass the final course exam with a minimum score of 80%.

This course is six hours in length.

Learning objektives[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1#learning-objektives)

Upon completion of this training, you will be able to:

· Describe ePO and the Trellix Agent.

· Install and upgrade ePO.

· Deploy and configure products to endpoints.

· Configure the ePO server.

· Create and manage policies and rules.

· Manage ePO user accounts and permission sets.

· Create and interpret ePO dashboards, queries, and reports.

· Describe the Disaster Recovery feature and how it works.

· Explain how to perform basic troubleshooting on ePO.

The Security Connected model drives how the company delivers and looks at security.

In this module, you will learn about applications and tools to help you better understand the threat landscape, vulnerabilities, and relevant countermeasures, translating into more effective risk management. You will also learn about ePO solutions basics, solution components, and key features along with how ePO fits in the Security Connected model.

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

· Identify ePO components, architecture, and communications

· Navigate within the ePO console

· Describe the ePO Single Sign-On feature

· Explain the purpose, key features, and functions of the Trellix Agent

· Describe the basic functionality available from the Trellix Agent system tray icon

# Communications: Tomcat Service | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

The Application Server (Tomcat Service) provides the most tangible services of the ePO core components.

· It provides the front end of the console’s user interface for management tasks and standardized database interface and handles application features, such as System Tree organization, user management, policy management, dashboards, and more.

· It runs the Notification System and supports the interactions between endpoints and ePO through extensions. Extensions are special software files that are supplied in a zipped format and are installed on the ePO server. They contain static files necessary for ePO to manage other endpoint security products. Examples: Endpoint Security (ENS) and Rogue Detection System (RSD).

· In addition, registered server types are added using extensions. Once the registered server types are added, users can register their servers with another ePO server for multi-server functions, such as shared policies.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F2cySQbD4cHfPsF0t0iEI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d4cb9ad-4047-4ffd-84c5-8251acad4aa2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87349e99&sv=2)

# How it Works | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

rellix security software and ePO work together to stop malware attacks on your systems and notify you when they occur. During an attack, ePO components and processes stop an attack, notify you when it occurs, and record the incident.

Click on the numbers below to see what happens during an attack.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FABGfbQY55ZRYRR3k52rg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daca0cfa9-0a8b-4c84-9936-dd56f5dc3fc9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5d421e3&sv=2)

# Communications: Security Keys | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

Security keys are used to verify, authenticate, and encrypt communications and content within your ePO-managed environment. The ePO server relies on three security key pairs to verify and authenticate communications and content within your ePO environment. These security key pairs are used to:

· Authenticate agent‑server communication

· Verify the contents of local repositories

· Verify the contents of remote repositories

Each key pair has:

· A secret key that signs messages or packages at the source

· A public key that verifies the messages or packages at the target

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fk5KYrsJX1LyKL5oPk3uj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41958746-e5e5-47a3-92cc-0352be66942d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d661a1ba&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FZ2l4LoDvVNh6fj7SVE71%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D354a5a40-8b22-4492-8412-66c8ccf5cb30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f355bb28&sv=2)

# Product Overview | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

The Trellix Agent is the client-side component of ePO. You must install it on each system in your network that you want ePO to manage.

Key functions:

· Provides a secure communication channel to ePO and local services for other point-products

· Includes an updater component that uses the Sitelist.XML file (list of available repositories) to find and download client or endpoint product updates; it can retrieve files from Hypertext Transfer Protocol (HTTP) sites, File Transfer Protocol (FTP) sites, Universal Naming Convention (UNC) shares, and ePO repositories. The order of sites in the site list controls the site chosen to do downloads. The updater attempts to get files from sites at the top of the list first. If it cannot get the files from the first site (perhaps because the site is down or the files it wants aren't there or are corrupted), it goes to the next one in order, and so on.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Feekii1qODHcOeZUtGSf0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21d2c6d2-ec9c-4dba-ae6a-c907a24fddd8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79fe0973&sv=2)

In addition to providing a secure communication channel, the Agent provides local services to managed Trellix products and to products developed by Trellix Security Innovation Alliance partners. While running silently in the background, the Agent:

· Gathers information and events from managed systems and sends them to the ePO server.

· Installs products and their upgrades on managed systems.

· Enforces policies and schedules tasks on managed systems.

· Updates security content, such as the DAT files associated with Endpoint Security or Host Intrusion Prevention.

The Agent uses Hypertext Transfer Protocol (HTTP) over an IP connection to communicate and uses TCP Port 80 or 443 by default, except for Agent Wakeup calls. Agent Wakeup calls use Transmission Control Protocol (TCP) Port 8081. Except for wakeup calls, the Agent initiates all communication between the ePO server and client. This communication is called the Agent-to-Server-Communication-Interval (ASCI).

[PreviousTrellix Agent Overview](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview)
[NextKey Features](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview/key-features)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

There are two categories of ePO software installations: a new installation in an environment where no previous version of ePO software has been installed and an upgrade where you are replacing an existing version of ePO software. Before you install your ePO server software, it is important to know which method you plan to use and have a solid understanding of the corresponding workflow, requirements, and procedures.

In this module you will learn about ePolicy Orchestrator installations.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Identify installation requirements, recommendations, and best practices
    
*   Describe the Pre-Installation Auditor tool functionality
    
*   Install and upgrade the ePO software
    
*   Perform post-installation tasks
    
*   Identify configuration tools for the initial setup of the ePO environment
    
*   Identify the upgrade checklist tasks

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   The ePO server can be fine-tuned to the needs of an organization through entries available in the Server Settings.
    
*   Agent Handlers distribute network traffic via agent-to-server communication interval (ASCI).
    
*   The System Tree contains all the systems managed by ePO.
    
*   You can group systems based on machine-type, geography, political boundaries, or any other logical criteria that supports your needs.
    
*   ePO offers two System Tree synchronization features: NT Domain Integration, and Active Directory Synchronization.
    
*   Tags can be used to identify and sort systems, simplify the creation of tasks and queries, and tailor reports to be more meaningful.
    
*   Use the Tag Catalog page to view summary information for any tag, begin creating or editing tags, and run sorting criteria.
    
*   You organize tags within the Tag Group Tree in a hierarchical structure, similar to ePO System Tree structure.
    

* * *

In the next lesson, you will learn how to deploy software manually and automatically in ePO.

* * *

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   You will need to use a SQL Server as the ePO database. Launch SQL Server Configuration Manager and verify the following before installing ePO: - Verify that the SQL Server service is running. - Verify TCP/IP is enabled.
    
*   Follow best practices for installing ePO software
    
*   The Pre-Installation Auditor now runs automatically as part of the installation process to validate that your existing configuration is ready for the upgrade.
    
*   After the installation is complete, connect to the ePO server and verify the ePO console is accessible.

# Tag Management | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/tag-management#tag-catalog)

**Tag Catalog**

Tags and tag groups allow you to select groups of systems and simplify the creation of tasks and queries. Some uses of tags are:

*   Automatic placement in System Tree groups
    
*   System Identification
    
*   Unique update and scan tasks for specific groups
    
*   Extra monitoring oversight and extra attention
    
*   Custom policies for specific systems/groups
    
*   Inclusion of selected system information in reports
    

The Tag Catalog is accessed from the Menu page (**Menu** \> **Systems** \> **Tag Catalog)**. The page has two basic parts: Tag Group Tree and Tags.

*   **Tag Group Tree** (left pane): Displays tags grouped by a hierarchical tree of groups and subgroups.
    
*   **Tags** (right pane): Tags help you identify and sort systems. The tag list displays the tags available for use. There typically are default Server and Workstation tags.
    

Use this page to view summary information for any tag, begin creating or editing tags, and run sorting criteria.

_**Click on the information (i) icons for further information.**_

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FVBwquZzcVk2WuPPm4gdO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0cd5e424-2f35-44a1-b4c7-330d6d4fa592&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdea7051&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/tag-management#tag-permissions)

**Tag Permissions**

To create or edit tags, or to apply, exclude and clear tags, you must have the appropriate permissions selected in the Systems Permission Set. Administrators have these rights by default, but other administrative users may need these permissions enabled on the Permission Sets page (**Menu** \> **User Management** > **Permission Sets**).

Since the Tag Builder accesses the Criteria definition page for a tag regardless if you use it, you will need to give anyone who will be creating tags the ability to use tag criteria, as displayed in this slide, as well as access to the **Create and edit private queries** set within the permission set.

The ePO administrator can also restrict usage of tags to available Permission Sets. This can be handy for administrators to help identify & sort systems accordingly in their environments.

By default, Tags are set to “**Do not restrict by Permission Sets**”.

To access & configure Tag Permissions, open the **Tag Catalog**, click on the desired Tag, and expand the **Restrictions** entry under the _Tag Details_ section.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FWFN21rs8Rb5Z5e0kqxC5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df007d97e-693c-48ca-b234-9e480aac6e9f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f30bbea&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FPnvj9WmnNQisqa8qCiBL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf9e25cc-4adc-41a2-82ff-b90c0f10a3dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb391264&sv=2)

> The ePO administrator can also restrict usage of tag to available Permission Sets. This can be handy for administrators to help identify and sort systems accordingly in their environments.
> 
> By default, Tags are set to “**Do not restrict by Permission Sets**”.
> 
> To access and configure Tag Permissions, open the **Tag Catalog**, click on the desired Tag, and expand the **Restrictions** entry under the _Tag Details_ section.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/tag-management#tag-actions-in-the-system-tree)

**Tag Actions in the System Tree**

Using the Tag **Actions** in the System Tree, you can manually apply tags to systems, clear tags from systems, and exclude system from automatic tagging.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FlWSOUVufhKFKsvPOy7hO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D414dc7f2-6095-4b95-b891-5ebf8d964e09&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40f4894f&sv=2)

> *   **Apply Tag**: Allows you to manually apply tags to systems
>     
> *   **Clear Tag**: Allows you to manually clear tags applied to systems
>     
> *   **Exclude Tag**: Allows you to exclude systems from having specific tags applied. Alternatively, you can use a query to collect systems, then, from the query results, you can exclude those tags from those systems.
>     

**Creating a Tag Demonstration**

[PreviousSystem Tree](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree)
[NextModule Summary](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/module-summary)

# Upgrade | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#changes-with-epo-5.10-service-pack-1)

**Changes with ePO 5.10 Service Pack 1**

ePO 5.10 Update 15 is the latest update in the initial series of cumulative updates (CUs) for ePO 5.10. The next release after that may have two different packages. Cumulative update indicates any update that is applied using the ePO 5.10 update tool.

*   **ePO 5.10 Service Pack 1** (ePO 5.10 SP1): This package can be used to install ePO for the first time and includes the updates in CU 1-15. It is also used to upgrade some versions of ePO 5.9.1 and earlier to ePO 5.10 SP1.
    
*   **ePO 5.10 Service Pack 1 Update** (ePO 5.10 SP1 CU): This package can be used to upgrade an existing ePO 5.10 server to service pack 1. _You do not need to install this if you have already installed ePO 5.10 Service Pack 1_.
    

EPO 5.10 SP1 Update is the last update to support both upgrading from and rolling back to ePO 5.10 CU 1–15. The update numbering then resets so that the next release after ePO 5.10 SP1 might be ePO 5.10 SP1 Update 1 (ePO 5.10 SP1 CU1), and so on. If you are on ePO 5.10 Update 15 or earlier, you must first apply ePO 5.10 SP1 CU before upgrading to ePO 5.10 SP1 CU1 or later.

**See** [**KB96141** (opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB96141)
**for the full list of upgrade paths supported for ePO - On-prem 5.10 Service Pack 1.**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FKsK7JtMuxchjdHCd1nTq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ce1e856-9764-4f39-bccc-7ad44a7cf7b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbcbff63&sv=2)

*   The upgrade path does not allow an upgrade from ePO 5.3.0 or earlier to ePO 5.10 SP1.
    
*   The Pre-Installation Auditor (embedded in the ePO 5.10 installer) verifies the ePolicy Orchestrator and SQL Database readiness for upgrade to ePO 5.10.
    
*   The Pre-Installation Auditor utility provides remediation steps for any conflicts found.
    
*   The Pre-Installation Auditor utility file (ePIP.exe) is also provided in the extracted folder and can be executed outside of the ePO installer file (setup.exe).
    

**After upgrading to ePO 5.10, you might need to rebuild indexes if index fragmentation gets too high or the built-in task fails to rebuild those indexes. Rebuilding the indexes is beneficial for better ePO performance. See** [**KB87769** (opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB87769)
**for details.**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#upgrading-epo-checklist)

**Upgrading ePO Checklist**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#plan-the-upgrade)

**Plan the Upgrade**

*   Read the release notes.
    
*   Review Knowledge Base articles for ePO:
    
    *   Known Issues: [KB90382(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB88906)
        
    *   Upgrade Paths: [KB86693(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB86693)
        
    *   Upgrade Paths for Service Pack 1 (SP1): [KB96141(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB96141)
        
    *   Minimum Supported Extensions/Versions: [KB94079(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB94079)
        
    *   Policy & System Migration: [KB88822(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB88822)
        
    
*   Gather required information: Grant Number License Key Database server and Database name DB Server credentials Primary administrator account credentials for ePO Keystore encryption passphrase
    
*   The Pre-Installation Auditor runs in installer by default.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#prepare-the-environment)

**Prepare the Environment**

*   Perform any updates as recommended by the Pre-Installation Auditor for the ePO server.
    
*   Back up ePO databases and directories.
    
*   Update registered server certificates.
    
*   Disable Trellix Agent installation tasks set to Run Immediately.
    
*   Disable scheduled server tasks and Windows tasks.
    
*   Disable third-party software.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#prepare-sql-database)

**Prepare SQL Database**

*   Perform any updates for the SQL Server as recommended by the Pre-Installation Auditor assessment of the SQL database.
    
*   Update your Windows Server to the latest Microsoft Service Packs and hotfixes.
    
*   Make sure that IPv6 is enabled.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#perform-the-upgrade)

**Perform the Upgrade**

Download and extract the software[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#download-and-extract-the-software)

Download the ePO software to your Windows Server.

Stop automatic updates[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#stop-automatic-updates)

Disable Windows updates to ensure they do not interfere with your ePO installation or upgrade.

Stop remote Agent Handlers services before upgrading[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#stop-remote-agent-handlers-services-before-upgrading)

If you use remote Agent Handlers in your environment, you must stop two services on each remote Agent Handler server to successfully complete your upgrade.

Stop ePO services[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#stop-epo-services)

Make sure that the Apache Tomcat service stops.

Start and complete the InstallShield wizard[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#start-and-complete-the-installshield-wizard)

Use Setup.exe to upgrade your ePO server.

Upgrade your remote Agent Handlers[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#upgrade-your-remote-agent-handlers)

When you upgrade your ePO server software, you must manually reinstall the Agent Handler software on any remote Agent Handlers installed throughout your environment. Agent Handlers are not automatically updated to the latest version when the ePO server is upgraded.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#restart-process-and-verify-upgrade)

**Restart Process and Verify Upgrade**

To remediate vulnerabilities in your ePO environment, migrate SHA-1 certificates to SHA-2 or higher; refer to [KB87017(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB87017)
.

Verify the upgrade:

1.  Run a query or server task.
    
2.  Perform an Agent wake-up call with one or more managed systems.
    
3.  Verify registered servers are communicating with the ePO server.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#migrate-sha-1-certificates-to-sha-2-or-higher)

**Migrate SHA-1 Certificates to SHA-2 or Higher**

The Certificate Manager allows you to:

*   Migrate certificates that are signed by older signing algorithm to the new algorithm, such as SHA-1 to SHA-256
    
*   Regenerate your certificates when your existing certificates are compromised due to vulnerabilities in your environment
    
*   Migrate or regenerate certificates for managed products that are derived from McAfee ePO root CA
    

This task replaces certificates that are used for all these ePO operations:

*   Agent-server communication
    
*   Authenticating to browsers
    
*   Certificate-based user authentication
    

**Read the instructions carefully before proceeding with the steps. If you activate the new certificates before they are populated on the systems in your network, those systems will not be able to connect to your ePO server, until the agents on those systems are re-installed**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#card-title-22)

Using Certificate Manager

The Certificate Manager page provides information about the installed Root Certificate, Agent Handler certificates, server certificates, and other certificates that are derived from ePO root Certificate Authority (CA).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FaY4gLh8gktQIvkWv858J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19b0be46-d273-489c-abbe-62d76c8e2647&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebe0512c&sv=2)

Log on as an administrator, then click **Menu** \> **Configuration** \> **Certificate Manager**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FTLsDI5hP2BoMIKP1b4he%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ceef781-15c2-4d96-ba5b-67c1693bb47e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59585a22&sv=2)

Click **Regenerate Certificate**

.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FEQ50EaNJNL1IN5EkQ2XP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D872dedce-5abd-41b9-ba55-56ef8ff949ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83ab74ef&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FM0OIEBj0J21riS1YeIxd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe66d5d1-3f80-4dfd-87a0-0e6a9f4dde51&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2962d25c&sv=2)

After the certificates regenerate, wait for sufficient saturation of the new certificates throughout your environment. As agents communicate to the ePO server, they are given the new certificate. The percentage of agents that have received the newly-generated certificates is provided in the **Certificate Manager** under **Product**: **Agent Handler** > **Status**. This distribution percentage is based on the number of agent-server communications that have occurred since the certificates were regenerated. Unmanaged inactive systems will affect this percentage.

**Note**: Make sure that the distribution percentage is as close to 100% as possible before you continue; otherwise, any pending systems will not receive the newly generated certificates and will be unable to communicate with ePO after the certificates are activated. You can stay in this state for as long as is necessary to achieve sufficient saturation.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FwpqkwgBY3Tohr46pBUSq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb46e4c2-bd9e-4405-8bb8-f6bbd6dbe9d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1dd0961a&sv=2)

1.  Once you've achieved a distribution percentage close to 100%, click **Activate Certificates** to carry out all future operations using the new certificates. A backup of the original certificates is created, and a message appears.
    
2.  Click **OK**. You must reinstall any agents that still use the old certificates to restore agent-to-server communication.
    

Once activation of certificates is complete, perform these steps:

1.  Stop the Agent Handler services (including the Remote Agent Handler services).
    
2.  Restart the ePO services.
    
3.  Start the Agent Handler services.
    

Monitor your environment and make sure that your agents are successfully communicating. You can cancel the migration at this point to roll back the certificate and restore agent-to-server communication; however, **after you’ve completed the next step, you can no longer cancel the certification migration**.

Click **Finish Migration** to complete the certificate migration. The certificate backup, taken during activation, is deleted.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#card-title-31)

Summary

For any issues during the migration, click **Cancel Migration** to revert to the previous certificates. If you cancel the migration, stop the Agent Handler services, restart the ePO service, and start the Agent Handler service again. You can start the certificate migration again after fixing any issues.

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/upgrade#undefined)

# ePO Console | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

Access the ePO console using a web browser.

**Design and Layout**

The ePO interface uses a menu-based navigation model and includes a navigation bar. The first menu in the bar is the one used when you log in to ePO. The default is Dashboards unless you have installed Protection Workspace. By default, the navigation bar includes access to these pages: Protection Workspace (if installed), Dashboards, System Tree, Support Center, Trellix ePO - SaaS Migration, Queries & Reports, Policy Catalog, and Security Resources. It also provides a new updates/notifications icon and a User Quick Access menu to let you log off the ePO console, view online help, and get support.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F5FFeA0Z2dLH33tF9k4OE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D138537c6-4cca-4e47-afb2-ea0da2feb051&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7405bc48&sv=2)

**Customizing the Navigation Bar**

You have the flexibility to customize the navigation bar for quick access to the features and functionality you use most often. You can decide which features are displayed on the navigation bar by dragging any menu item on or off the navigation bar. The features displayed in the navigation bar are stored as user preferences, so each user’s customized navigation bar displays regardless of which console they use to log on to the server.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FI1mSgGgNzETyXnxTdVNz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db34b2297-db71-4f92-99ae-4307d598c503&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bd0b74f&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FowoueMm3tbQMFO9icxx0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da86e383c-2610-45b1-b9de-ce2f5bba7df9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74023497&sv=2)

**Menu Page**

Click the **Menu** (three line stack) icon on the navigation bar to go to the Menu page.

The Menu page provides a central launching point for all ePO pages. The Menu organizes the pages by category and includes links to the subpages for the category; for example, to manage users, go to the User Management category and then click the Users link.

As you add new managed products to your server, the associated interface pages are either added to an existing category, or a new category is added to the Menu page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FX0htXxn0dLvybEP8BPlO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf107417-25dd-41e5-9048-b3d3336be3e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e55b77e&sv=2)

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

ePO simplifies the process of deploying products to the managed systems in your network by providing a user interface to configure and schedule deployments.

In this module, you will learn how to deploy software manually and automatically.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Explain how the Software Catalog works
    
*   Install extensions and software components using the Software Catalog
    
*   Install extensions and software components manually
    
*   Create a Product Deployment Project
    
*   Deploy software to endpoints through the Client Task Catalog
    
*   Describe the purpose of client tasks
    
*   Access and navigate the Client Task Catalog

# Services | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

Trellix Agent provides these services:

· Trellix Agent Service: Performs property collection, policy enforcement, schedules tasks, performs agent-server communication, and triggers the update session

o Service name: Masvc

o Windows processes: masvc.exe

o Non-Windows processes: masvc

· Trellix Agent Common Services: Hosts multiple Trellix Agent services, such as Peer-to-Peer, Wake-up, and RelayServer

o Service name: Macmnsvc

o Windows processes: macmnsvc.exe

o Non-Windows processes: macmnsvc

· Trellix Agent Backwards Compatibility Service: The Trellix Agent service starts this service and communicates to the various managed product plugins. You only see this when the executable is invoked.

o Service name: McAfee Framework

o Windows processes: macompatsvc.exe

o Non-Windows processes: macompatsvc

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FhQuVb2qlMdBZwNwuaySx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D052fe4d2-99e3-43bf-9f53-cd44b8948e74&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1497491&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FlNXXzLn4tT2dISI6WndN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D477380a7-7bf5-4081-ad6c-2a67776a1384&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7d9fcba&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F4SBY1ECYYk6vtzRpxH0n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d299442-635c-4745-9c70-b46cb87d1d7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54f23504&sv=2)

First Tab

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview/services#tab-first-tab)

Second Tab

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview/services#tab-second-tab)

On Windows client systems, the install logs are saved in **%TEMP%\\McAfeeLogs**.

Log files can be found in these locations, depending on the managed system’s operating system:

1.  On Windows client
    
2.  systems: <Documents and Settings>\\All Users\\Application Data\\McAfee\\ Agent\\Logs
    
3.  If no Documents and Settings folder:<ProgramData>\\McAfee\\Agent\\Logs
    
4.  On non-Windows client systems: /var/McAfee/agent/logs
    

**Using the System Tray Icon**

In a Windows environment, if the Agent policy is set to show the Agent icon in the system tray of the managed system, you can access shortcuts to information and functionality of managed products.

**Update Security**

–

Triggers immediate updating of all installed Trellix software products. This includes application of patches and hotfixes, as well as DAT and signature updates. Note this feature is available only if specifically enabled in the Agent policy.

**Quick Settings**

–

Links to product menu items that are frequently used

**Manage Features**

–

Displays links to the administrative console of managed products

**Scan Computer for**

–

Launches Trellix programs, such as Endpoint Security, that scan systems on-demand and detect unwanted malicious software

**View Security Status**

–

Displays the current system status of managed Trellix products, including current events

**Agent Status Monitor**

–

Triggers the Agent Status Monitor, which:

*   Displays information on the collection and transmission of properties
    
*   Sends events
    
*   Downloads and enforces policies
    

**About**

–

Displays system and product information for products installed on the system, including the Agent, the ePO server with which the Agent communicates, and the software products being managed

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FqdWShBRqiNqsbZ8KC4aJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a6478d6-0f07-4e3a-a438-5256a24b4637&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bf958cb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview/services#forcing-trellix-agent-activity)

Forcing Trellix Agent Activity

There are two methods available to force communications to occur from a managed client to the ePO server: opening the Trellix Agent Status Monitor and using the command line.

**Open the Trellix Agent Status Monitor**

If the ePO icon displays in the Windows system tray, open the Agent Monitor. The following options are available:

· **Collect and Send Props**: Forces the Agent to collect machine and product properties configuration and communicate them to the ePO server. **Note**: The Agent policy controls whether full or incremental properties are sent to the ePO server.

· **Send Events**: Forces the Agent to send events to the ePO server. Note: This action sends all events to the ePO server irrespective of their severity.

· **Check New Policies**: Forces the Agent to communicate with the ePO server and check for the existence of updated policies; will also update any modified or newly created tasks.

· **Enforce Policies**: Forces the Agent to read the local copy of the ePO policy and enforce this on the machine.

· **Agent Settings**: Configures Trellix Agent settings and Network Settings

· **Save Contents to Desktop**: Saves the contents of the Trellix Agent log to a file

· **Close**: Closes the Trellix Agent Monitor window

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FpGQdERSl7TkK1JErwvle%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4484a047-3f65-4cb2-ae25-56d469705107&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61538002&sv=2)

Note that you can see the Agent icon in the system tray only if the Show system tray icon (Windows only) option is selected on the General tab of the Trellix Agent policy pages. If you cannot see the icon, select this option and apply it. When you finish viewing the log file content, you can hide the icon again by deselecting the option and applying the change.

Use the Command Line

When the Agent is installed, an executable (CMDAGENT.EXE) is also installed in the Agent directory (<Drive>:\\Program Files\\Trellix\\Common Framework, by default). This command line utility lets you to execute Agent commands without using the Trellix Agent Status Monitor. Switches allow you to specify the action(s) the Agent undertakes and are equivalent to the options provided by the Trellix Agent Status Monitor:

· **Collect and Send Properties and Events: CMDAGENT.EXE /p**

**· Check New Policies: CMDAGENT.EXE /c**

**· Enforce Policies: CMDAGENT.EXE /e**

**· Show Agent monitor: CMDAGENT.EXE /s**

**· Forward events from Windows based client systems to ePO server: CMDAGENT.EXE /f**

**· Displays the agent information: CMDAGENT.EXE /i**

**· Sets the logfile location: CMDAGENT.EXE -l**

**· Displays the help information**: CMDAGENT.EXE /h

· **Forward events from Unix based and Macintosh client systems to ePO server: CMDAGENT /f**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FFE2Ctuqa23DP5gll4inh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52476582-9574-4800-8e3c-d6c8b2d8801c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63b00026&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F8pSasIfhXVq8n80ljZGm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a2fc6c-07b3-4205-a44a-f7bb3d95ef90&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=680b37b0&sv=2)

[PreviousKey Features](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/trellix-agent-overview/key-features)
[NextePO Resources](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-overview/epo-resources)

# Software Catalog | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/software-catalog#software-catalog-user-interface)

**Software Catalog User Interface**

The Software Catalog informs you about the availability of new and updated licensed software products that your organization uses, as well as trial (evaluation) versions. It also lets you check in, update, and remove many managed product components from the ePO server.

Software availability and whether it is in the Licensed or Evaluation category depends on your license key. Some components, such as Help extensions or those made up of MSI installers, cannot be installed using this action. You must download and manually install these types of components.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FLPzj5KnZqmSqnXq1BrxT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7975b302-cb0c-4927-9032-e0660da140b8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d472059&sv=2)

**Your ePO server must have Internet access because it connects to the download server to verify which products are available.**

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/software-catalog#card-title-2)
> 
> Package/Extension Check-in
> 
> From the Software Catalog, you can download, check in, update, and remove managed product components from your server.
> 
> To download software or product documentation to a location on your network and check in a product package or extensions to your ePO server, complete these steps from the Software Catalog.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fc1zNzaupnTgF2vCECwbN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e620a04-991a-4adf-9ea6-837b829d0fff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3094a85f&sv=2)

Select **Menu** \> **Software** \> **Software Catalog** to open the Software Catalog page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FUQK8HhSUzKcTaWsPikdN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bcb985b-53f9-4a99-9d19-ec2c0df45e0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50db0d42&sv=2)

Click on the desired category entry under **Products**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FZdTYenED2d9BGjClBE8I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D394a8b78-6e60-45c1-8935-bd1a5be857ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8379b511&sv=2)

In the table in the right pane, select (highlight) a product/type, such as **Trellix Data Exchange Layer 6.0**. In this case, you can expand the product and select the extension or package you wish to install (for example, DXL Broker 6.0.3).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F2zmIzCYXAS0bfFM9kXN1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D856e86d4-f111-47e4-a9f4-b5406c84dc1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd38e6ac&sv=2)

In the details pane to the far-right, click **Check In** under **Actions**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FlyVJYKVN9B6HEr0r8oHm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0cdc996-cc0b-4bfc-b1d0-afa497a41a58&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=598694f3&sv=2)

In the _Check In_ pane, review and accept the product details and End User License Agreement (EULA).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FeDuFEYG5g4IWzbc9VSsE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df110da98-1d68-44bb-a794-a9143d36e7a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e448a27&sv=2)

If you are checking in a package, in the _Check In Options_ pane, select the desired branch.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FO5J5SzkCMNupTydWSbAN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f6acdf1-bc89-4eed-a911-1369ef32cf1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ead6204d&sv=2)

Click **Check In**.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/software-catalog#card-title-10)

Verifying Package/Extension Check-in

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FwJiQVw7IBgN2XME8X8wE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df71f5734-5143-42ed-acfd-218ac20297b8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8669448a&sv=2)

To verify the task completed successfully once the check-in completes, click the product entry again under the Software Catalog <category> pane and do the following:

1.  Compare the _**Available Version**_ against the _**Check in Version**_ entry.
    
2.  To see details for the task, expand **Actions** and click **View Task Log**.
    

**To update a package or extension, follow the same steps as you would for check-in, but instead of choosing** _**Check in**_ **under Actions, choose** _**Update**_**. If you wish to remove a package or extension, choose** _**Remove**_ **under Actions.**

# Pre-Installation Auditor Tool | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

When you install or upgrade to ePO 5.10 or later, the ePO Pre-Installation Auditor (PIA) utility is integrated into the installer and enabled by default. The PIA tool helps to reduce or prevent installation or upgrade issues.

The auditor automates many of the verification tasks included in the installation or upgrade process to make sure your environment meets the minimum requirements. Additionally, ePO Pre-Installation Auditor allows you to change your ePO Admin password.

The ePO Pre-Installation Auditor utility performs many checks, from confirming ePO and SQL Server hardware requirements to various SQL database compatibility checks. For detailed information on all of the checks this tool performs, see the Pre-Installation Auditor section in the ePO 5.10 Installation Guide.

If you need to run the ePO Pre-Installation Auditor utility outside of the installer, follow these steps:

1.  The ePO Pre-Installation Auditor tool is located within the ePO 5.10 Installation files under the **ePOIP** folder. Double-click **ePIP.exe** to start the auditor, then follow the prompts.
    
2.  Once all checks have passed, click **Finish**.
    

For details on known issues with ePolicy Orchestrator Pre-Installation Auditor, see [KB88906(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB88906)
.

Additionally, review [KB87017 (opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB87017)
carefully to avoid a possible disruption in agent-to-server communication.

**ePO Installation Preparation**

**Best Practices**

*   Install latest Microsoft updates.
    
*   Update the ePO database server with the latest Microsoft security updates for the database software you use.
    
*   Ensure ports to be used by ePO are available.
    
*   If Endpoint Security (ENS) is installed, disable Access Protection and stop ENS services.
    
*   After ePO installation, install firewall software (for example, ENS) on the ePO server.
    
*   Update your software with the most current intrusion detection signature files.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#prerequisites)

**Prerequisites**

Local administrator account credentials[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#local-administrator-account-credentials)

An account with local administrator permissions is required to log on to the Windows server computer to be used as the ePO server.

Product License Key[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#product-license-key)

If you don't have a license key, you can select **Evaluation** to continue installing the software. The evaluation period is limited to 90 days. You can provide a license key after installation is complete from within the application. For more information, see the product guide or Help.

Authentication credentials[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#authentication-credentials)

Supports Windows and SQL authentication.

*   **Microsoft Windows authentication**: Credentials for a domain administrator user account
    
*   **SQL authentication**: Required SQL Server permissions (Discussed later in this module)
    

Destination folder[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#destination-folder)

Folder for ePO software, if different than the default (C:\\Program Files (86)\\Trellix \\ePolicy Orchestrator\\)

Supported SQL Server[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#supported-sql-server)

It is important to know if you plan to install SQL Server or plan to use a manually installed or existing SQL server.

SQL Server details[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#sql-server-details)

*   Name of the SQL Server (This name should be formatted using the SQL Server name or the SQL Server name with instance name.)
    
*   Dynamic port number used by your SQL Server
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/pre-installation-auditor-tool#downloading-epo-software)

**Downloading ePO Software**

A grant number is required to obtain ePO software and documentation from Product Download Site ([**https://www.trellix.com/en-us/downloads/my-products.html**(opens in a new tab)](https://www.trellix.com/en-us/downloads/my-products.html)
).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FXpfDdHskhXMQo7bRRBfN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8b90df0-1bd0-42d4-8f17-7e99f2be2ded&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=772f32d9&sv=2)

Click on **Download**, and the screen below displays.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F3d9iN0c7gAzw5ZwtZQRy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a4eb85e-7775-46bd-9098-6930d00d4db2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=973e2d74&sv=2)

**Installing ePO Software**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FfeOY8nXc8SPx2B1ctvpr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f49b6bc-86e3-40a7-9628-0e8d8e83728c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b33611d6&sv=2)

1.  From the ePO server, extract your ePO software files to a temporary directory, then browse to the temporary directory and double click on the Setup icon (Setup.exe), or select **File** \> **Open**. Wait while the program prepares for the install. Do not attempt to run Setup.exe without first extracting the .zip file. **Note**: You may be alerted about RAM or monitor requirements. With ePO 5.10, 8 GB available RAM minimum is recommended. The monitor should be 1024x768, 256-color, VGA.
    
2.  Click **OK** to continue.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FDoqylfdJIrQmupttSaaV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f1727cd-28dd-4bfb-9e5c-c74d8e5174a0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca681ff0&sv=2)

1.  A welcome window opens. Read the information on the window, then click **Next** to begin.
    
2.  If any prerequisite software is needed, click **Next** to install the software. Wait while the software is installed.
    

**Note**: Disregard the _Restore_ option as it does not apply to a new install. The restore option is used to quickly recover if the hardware hosting your ePO server fails. It saves your ePO configuration, extensions, keys, and more to Snapshot records in the ePO database.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FTlT1mXB8Y4Msd4aJmrKw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9609249c-e1c7-4411-93d1-9406e4b83e70&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fcef4fe&sv=2)

In the Destination Folder step, click:

*   **Next** to install the ePO software in the default location (C:\\Program Files (x86)\\Trellix\\ePolicy Orchestrator\\).
    
*   **Change** to specify a custom destination location for your ePO software. When the Change Current Destination Folder window opens, browse to the destination and create folders if needed. After specifying the new destination, click **Next** to continue.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FvjA2rUSq6GFnuGLAh3GD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b784595-a747-4a4d-8e15-81700c737bf3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=42106287&sv=2)

Complete the Database Information window, then click **Next**.

*   **Database Server**: Select from drop-down list.
    
*   **Database Name**: The Database Name is populated automatically.
    
*   **Database Server credentials**: Select and define the authentication type.
    
    *   **Windows authentication**: Select the domain of the user account to be used to access the SQL Server. If using a previously-installed SQL server, also type the User name and Password. If you are using a previously installed SQL Server, make sure your user account has access.
        
    *   **SQL authentication**: Type the User name and Password for your SQL Server. Make sure that the credentials you provide represent an existing user on the SQL Server, with appropriate rights.
        
    
*   **Username / Password**: Enter user name and password that ePO will use to connect to the SQL server.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Flw6a6OzMx2Kz0yRZHXHs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D540233da-e4bc-4ab4-9d1a-02da634a8df8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f144efa1&sv=2)

The Pre-Installation Auditor starts automatically and begins running checks to on all the components to determine compliance with requirements. A warning appears if the system does not pass all the checks. Click **OK** and resolve issues as needed, then click **Finish**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FRbmqtRbsPKw2NmBEW9qT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df616fbaa-afba-439e-869a-1a482909166a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a12d75b7&sv=2)

The ports that ePO uses are predefined and populated by default.

If a SQL Server is installed on the same server as ePO, then ePO uses the dynamically assigned port on a local SQL Server port. The port for the remote SQL server remains 1433. In the example, the local port assignment is shown.

After your installation is complete, you can change only the Agent wake‑up communication port and Agent broadcast communication port. If you need to change your other port settings later, reinstall your ePO software.

Refer to the Installation Guide on the dynamic ports that are assigned to the SQL Server by the SQL Server.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FjK1LlRwkIP7vfQbMgaSz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77f85a68-c713-4171-8b8b-c9adb42995dd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c3702c3&sv=2)

Complete the Administrator Information dialog, then click **Next**.

*   **Username / Password**: Enter the Username and Password for primary global administrator account.
    
*   **Keystore Encryption Passphrase**: Enter passphrase (8-20 characters). Required for Disaster Recovery.
    

After installation, you can reset the Keystore Encryption Passphrase from the Server Settings page (**Menu** \> **Server Settings** > **Disaster Recovery** > **Edit**).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FEnbDPHwv1yS7jIxRqcaN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc026edb2-fdbf-4f7a-b63b-b1945ac71d32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c9d0d5c&sv=2)

Enter the **License Key** or select **Evaluation**, then click **Next**. The evaluation period expires after 90 days.

**Automatic Product Configuration**

During an automatic configuration, your ePO server downloads and installs all the products entitled to you by your site license. In most cases, during an automatic configuration, you never see the Automatic Product Configuration process run. It starts running as soon as you finish installing the ePO software and is usually finished before you log on.

If the Automatic Product Configuration page appears when you initially log on to ePO, an error occurred while downloading or installing your products.

**Example**: If your Internet connection is interrupted.

Make a note of the product that failed to install and click **Retry** to attempt the product installation again.

To stop the automatic product installation, click **Stop**. A confirmation dialog box asks you to confirm that you want to use Software Manager to install your products.

**IMPORTANT**: Once you click **OK** in the **Stop Automatic Product Setup** confirmation dialog box, you must use the Software Manager to install your products. The Automatic Product Configuration is available only once during your initial configuration. If a product continues to fail during Automatic Product Configuration, contact Technical Support, or click **OK** to exit the Automatic Product Configuration page and begin setting up the ePO server. For future product installation status information, open the Software Manager (**Menu** \> **Software** \> **Software Manager**).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fs9hhEq6dT7cIvBFPlffE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5735c88e-d195-4a14-965b-c3d59333d5fd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899e46a2&sv=2)

1.  Accept the End User License Agreement to continue the installation. Optionally, change the location if different than United States. Click **OK** to continue.
    
2.  The Ready to Install the Program window appears. Optionally, disable the option to allow Trellix to collect system and software telemetry data, then click **Install**.
    

**Product Improvement Program** The Product Improvement Program collects the data from the client systems where Trellix products are installed and that are managed by ePO. It helps improve Trellix products.

The Product Improvement Program collects these types of data:

*   System environment (software and hardware details)
    
*   Effectiveness of installed Trellix product features
    
*   Trellix product errors and related Microsoft Windows events
    

Trellix product errors and related Microsoft Windows events The collected data is aggregated on the ePO server, then sent to the Product Improvement Program server once a day (default collection period) and stored at \\TelemetryData. Trellix uses the data that is collected by the program to analyze and improve the product experience for customers. The collected data is analyzed by Trellix to improve product features and customers' experiences with the product. It is also used by Trellix Technical Support for troubleshooting.

To learn about this program, click the **More Information** button. (Requires internet access).

**Privacy Protection** The collected data is used only for product improvement and technical support. The system-specific data is filtered or used in aggregate form, unless it is required for technical support.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FtVDwQKqn3kmwqqKirI4v%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D882e437c-0260-4089-9d2b-b844c59fd8b3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c9bb2dd8&sv=2)

1.  Wait while the installation program installs ePO. This may take some time.
    
2.  The InstallShield Wizard dialog appears after the installation is complete. Click **Finish**.
    

[PreviousInstallation and Upgrade](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/installation-and-upgrade)
[NextPost-Installation Tasks](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks)

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

In this module, you will learn about the default policies included with ePO, as well as the Policy Catalog organization and controls. You will learn how to create, assign, enforce, and share policies. You will also learn about policy inheritance, permission sets, and policy comparison.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/policy-management/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Describe the purpose of policies
    
*   Create and edit policy objects
    
*   Manage policy configuration and assignment
    
*   See policy inheritance in action
    
*   Enforce policy changes on client machines (endpoints)

# Product Deployment | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

ePO simplifies the process of deploying security products to the managed systems in your network, by providing a user interface to configure and schedule deployments.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fa7-br7FSQpqocEao_sr0CJOAnNS6kLZQq.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e33c4ad&sv=2)

There are three processes you can follow to deploy products using ePO.

Product Deployment Projects[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#product-deployment-projects)

Streamline the deployment process by consolidating many of the steps needed to create and manage product deployment tasks, individually. Provide more functionality than client tasks.

**Examples**: The ability to run a deployment continuously, stop a deployment, and uninstall a previously deployed product.

Client Tasks[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#client-tasks)

The Client Tasks Catalog applies the concept of logical objects to ePO client tasks. You can create client task objects for a variety of purposes, without the need to assign them immediately. As a result, you can treat these objects as reusable components when assigning and scheduling client tasks.

Install with an Installation URL[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#install-with-an-installation-url)

You can install the product on a local system with an installation URL. You can create a custom installation URL and use it to install the client software on your own local system or send it to end users to install the client software on their systems.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#product-deployment-project)

**Product Deployment Project**

The Product Deployment page is a single location, where you can create, monitor, and manage your product deployment projects.

_**Click on the information (i) icons to view additional information about each main part of the page.**_

![Product Deployment Project.png](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FLoU3k12jz-MUdfpt_zqqXSoBqrGC1widv.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4ec50d&sv=2)

1.  ![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FA4EkSNEtHn02tPRr3Gyd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54232144-8b86-4fcd-b4b8-4a03f36f15fa&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63047555&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#system-selection-continuous-deployment)

**System Selection: Continuous Deployment**

_Continuous deployments_ use System Tree groups or tags for the systems, which allows you to move systems to those groups or assign system tags, applying the deployment to those systems.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fn30kF3wYLg2UyBYf_TYvFP1OJmGxP3jBo.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7507e75b&sv=2)

**There is no limit to number of systems selected for a continuous deployment but be mindful of any bandwidth, implications with scheduling, etc.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#system-selection-fixed-deployment)

**System Selection: Fixed Deployment**

_Fixed_ deployments use a fixed or defined set of systems. System selection is done using your System Tree or Managed Systems Query output tables.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F9DA8HvvdsEgQ6X1Z_MA43oXO_8S1QoeFe.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d96c68a&sv=2)

**Limited to 500 systems in a Product Deployment Project. If more than 500 systems are selected, you will be prompted to select few systems.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#reviewing-product-deployments)

**Reviewing Product Deployments**

Audit logs from your deployment projects contain records of all product deployments made from the console, using the **Product Deployment** feature.

These audit log entries are displayed in a sortable table within the Deployment details area of the Product Deployment page, as well as on the Audit Log page, which contains log entries from all auditable user actions. You can use these logs to track, create, edit, duplicate, delete, and uninstall product deployments. Click a log entry to display entry details.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FZmv4HUlYk088miTG__g4WVrZnwN-mzMSb.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ebc220&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#client-task-catalog)

**Client Task Catalog**

Another way to deploy software products is using the Client Task Catalog.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FW7kSMRN8xYvSc7vd_9veeAEbYak8oKLEc.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4d5a9e&sv=2)

*   Assigned at any level in the System Tree
    
*   Inherited by groups and systems lower in the tree
    
*   Allows inheritance to be broken
    
*   Can be shared across multiple registered ePO servers
    
*   Must be assigned to managed systems
    
*   Can be scheduled to run or run immediately
    

**Product Deployment client tasks deploy products to your managed systems from the Main Repository. Product Update client tasks control when and how managed systems receive updates when global updating is not used. If you are not using global updating, client update tasks is the only way you can control client updating with ePO software.**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#using-the-main-repository-to-create-a-deployment-task)

**Using the Main Repository to Create a Deployment Task**

You can also create a deployment task from the Main Repository as shown below. Click the **Create Deployment Task** button to create a task.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F1ydQh8HSDKAfXjTc_WhNwOt_DORi8lNG2.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e1c6957&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#using-the-main-repository-to-create-a-deployment-task-workflow)

**Using the Main Repository to create a Deployment Task: Workflow**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FmslyVtfMzXuEjRpE_fJn5akOoFId0wmuD.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c1210d5&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#creating-an-installation-url)

**Creating an Installation URL**

Typically, ePO Cloud administrators create an installation URL that can be used to install Endpoint Security Client on managed systems. They can:

*   Use this URL to install the client software locally on their own system.
    
*   send this URL to users, with instructions for installing the client software on their local systems.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FjenRczulD6pocr7O_X-nz8VTxojlW8EER.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e2235a5d&sv=2)

1.  From the ePO console, select **Menu** \> **Dashboards**, then select **Getting Started with ePolicy Orchestrator** from the drop-down list.
    
2.  The products in the Main Repository, available to install on managed systems, are listed under **My Products**.
    
3.  Click the **Customize Installation** button and complete the required information.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/product-deployment#creating-an-installation-url-workflow)

**Creating an Installation URL: Workflow**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FvV7LRcc9ugurmdhE_y8tCjxI50FTjKhon.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a52294b0&sv=2)
