# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/policy-management/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   By default, only the administrator or creator can modify a policy. Policy ownership can be changed, and a policy can have multiple owners.
    
*   McAfee Default policy is read-only. My Default policy can be edited, renamed, duplicated, deleted, exported, and shared.
    
*   Create a custom policy by duplicating an existing one. By default, custom polices have no assignments.
    
*   A child inherits its parent’s settings unless inheritance is broken.
    
*   Policy assignment rules let you manage policies for multiple users or system based on specific criteria.
    
*   The Policy Comparison tool is used to compare policies that are similar, allowing you to determine which settings are different and which are the same.
    

In the next lesson, you will learn how to manage ePO users.

[PreviousDuplicating and Editing a Policy Simulation](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/policy-management/duplicating-and-editing-a-policy-simulation)
[NextModule Intro](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/module-intro)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Post-Installation Tasks | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

*   Verify services are installed/started.
    
*   bullet
    
    Make sure Startup type for SQL Server Agent (EPOSERVER) service is Automatic.
    
*   bullet
    
    Make sure pop-up blocker is off.
    
*   bullet
    
    Log in to ePO for first time.
    
*   bullet
    
    Import root certificate.
    
*   bullet
    
    Install required updates for Trellix security products (if appropriate).
    
*   bullet
    
    View port assignments.
    
*   bullet
    
    Configure ePO for multiple NICs (if appropriate).
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#verify-services-are-installed-and-started)

**Verify Services are Installed and Started**

1.  Select **Start** \> **Programs** \> **Administrative Tools** > **Services**.
    
2.  Identify the services installed on the server and started. Pay special attention to these services:
    
    1.  **Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator Application Server Service (Tomcat)**: Responsible for displaying the ePO console and running extensions, as well as other background functions.
        
    2.  **Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator Event Parser Service**: Takes events uploaded from clients in your environment and parses them into the SQL database.
        
    3.  **Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator Server Service (Apache)**: Processes and receives all agent-server communication.
        
    

**Log Files for Application Server**, **Event Parser**, and **Server Services** The following are the primary log locations for these services:

*   **Application Server service (Tomcat)**: orion.log or orion\_servername.log located in: ...\\<epoinstallationdirectory>\\server\\logs\\
    
*   **Event Parser service**: eventparser.log or eventparser\_servername.log located in: ..\\<epoinstallationdirectory>\\db\\logs\\
    
*   **Server service (Apache)**: server.log or server\_servername.log located in: ...\\<epoinstallationdirectory>\\db\\logs\\
    

**List of Services**

*   Trellix ePO Application Server Service (Tomcat)
    
*   Trellix ePO Event Parser Service
    
*   Trellix ePO Server Service (Apache)
    
*   Product Improvement Program Service (optional)
    
*   SQL Server
    
*   SQL Server Agent
    
*   SQL Server Browser
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FdLLMdoECwRwwqwJsajxL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb6c18e7-1efa-4ba2-9868-eafc3f009bfb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48b78636&sv=2)

Rely on constant, high-speed connection to ePO SQL Server database/ Cluster installs only

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#logging-in-to-epo-for-the-first-time)

**Logging in to ePO for the First Time**

After the installation is complete, connect to the ePO server and verify the ePO console is accessible. Because the console is web-based, you can also access the console remotely using a supported browser at one of these addresses:

*   https://<servername>:<console-to-server port (default 8443)
    
*   https://<ipaddress\_of\_server>:<console-to-server port (default 8443)
    

After connecting to the server, log in with default admin account credentials. These credentials are case-sensitive. (Later, you will add accounts for other ePO users.)

*   Preferred language (**Note**: Choose English UK as the language for European date and time format. )
    
*   User name: admin (default)
    
*   Password: as specified during the install
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FMpNBIax1eRXTKfO7Jn5w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2965fb58-081f-45c7-9a85-e347506cee11&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e70da3c4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#login-guidelines)

**Login Guidelines**

*   You can log on to multiple ePO servers by opening a new browser session or tab for each ePO server.
    
*   The computer must exist in the same domain, (or a domain that has a trust relationship with that domain) as the ePO server.
    
*   If a system name contains an underscore (\_) character, log on using the ePO server’s IP address, rather than the machine name.
    
*   Console communication is secured with industry standard Secure Socket Layer (SSL).
    
*   If desired, you can change the default login banner to meet your own needs. Click **Menu** \> **Configuration** \> **Server Settings**, select **Login Message** from the Settling Categories, then click **Edit**. Select **Display custom login message**, then enter your message and click **Save**.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#logging-in-to-epo-using-identity-provider)

**Logging in to ePO using Identity Provider**

ePO Single Sign-On feature enables the customer to bring their own identity provider for the user authentication purposes. This feature internally uses SAML (Security Assertion Markup Language) that allows identity providers (IdPs) to pass authorization credentials to service providers (SP).

Supported Identity Providers:

*   OKTA
    
*   ADFS
    
*   Ping Identity
    
*   Azure AD
    
*   Onelogin
    

The service provider will be ePO.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#card-title-14)

Install Trellix ePO Single Sign-On Extension

Follow this process to install the ePO Single Sign-On extension from the Trellix Download site using your Trellix Grant Number.

Prerequisites:

*   Trellix ePO version must be 5.10.0 Update 11 or later
    
*   Configure your Identity Provider application
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F2KP1WpgwZd1YKeIqUbUH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c1f6e34-a197-4b79-aadc-160654ef60e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9fe0a7fb&sv=2)

After entering your grant number, search for ePolicy Orchestrator and select version 5.10

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FqQNVGrVCihQDwTzLMMwu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60142036-1336-48b8-a8c9-04a8368ab2c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=881b6e0&sv=2)

In **Available Downloads**, select **Filters type** as **EXTENSION**, select ePO Single Sign-On version 1.0.0.xxx, and download it to your local ePO server.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F9QcEasX9lhtE58uZcssU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D474c516a-8d48-4df9-9907-d2c4254d0423&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d26ccb45&sv=2)

In ePO, go to **Menu** \> **Software** > **Extensions**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F91Dt0Y9bkV6goOZODqH9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f78efe4-d3ff-4332-b9d2-94f697f572cd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e58e298f&sv=2)

Click **Install Extension**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FwWuZiMABkluIth1pIrGD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D416cb157-9d1b-4001-b399-51921848e5be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7761747&sv=2)

Browse to and select the **ePOSingleSignOn\_release\_<version\_number>.<build\_number>.zip** extension file, click **Open**, then click **OK** twice.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#card-title-20)

Note

You can also download the extension from the Software Catalog of your ePO server.

**Configuring SSO to Log on to ePO**

Configuring the IdP Application[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#configuring-the-idp-application)

*   Configure a new IdP application in your SSO solution to get the IdP Entity Id (Issuer URL), IdP SSO URL, and X 509 certificate to input in your SAML configuration information
    
*   For instructions on how to configure your IdP application, see your identity provider’s documentation
    

**Note**: You might need to use placeholder information for the ACS URL and the Audience URI (Service Provider Entity ID) when you configure your third-party IdP. Enter the details when you Update your IdP application SAML settings with the information from the ePO server.

Input SAML Configuration Information[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#input-saml-configuration-information)

Configure the settings in the **IDP SAML Settings** page under **Server Settings** to enable SSO using your IdP application:

*   **Import IDP Metadata xml file** — Download the metadata from your IdP, and then click **Import** to upload the metadata to ePO
    
*   After entering the details, click **Save**
    
*   Once you log off from the ePO application, you will see the **Log On with IDP** option on the main screen
    

**Note**: Some IdPs do not support the download of the metadata extension. You will need to input data manually after collecting the necessary details from your IdP application.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FZFZBIwnGYe5ni9lWQR10%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29f339c0-3996-4d4c-91c9-de3591777f0f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e057d519&sv=2)

Update IdP Configuration with Information from ePO Server[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#update-idp-configuration-with-information-from-epo-server)

Edit SAML settings in your IdP application with information from ePO

1.  **Audience URL (Service Provider Entity ID)**: Enter the Service Provider (ePO) Entity ID from ePO
    
2.  **Single Sign On URL**: Enter the Service Provider Assertion Consumer Service URL from ePO
    

Assign the User Local for the IdP Application[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#assign-the-user-local-for-the-idp-application)

When logging in using an identity provider, the user locale is assigned in the following manner:

*   **From the user\_locale attribute**: It is configured in the IdP application to inform the Service Provider application about the locale of a particular user; for example: Fr-fr or, FR\_fr
    
*   **Using the drop-down option**: It is present on the logon screen of the ePO application
    
*   Available as the default locale of the tenant
    

**Using the Logon with IdP Feature**

1.  After configuration, click the Log On with IDP option on the ePO logon page (Service Provider initiated SSO), or click the configured application in the IdP console (Identity Provider initiated SSO), to test the logon option. On successful authentication, a page displays with the following message: _SAML authentication is successful_.
    
2.  Close your browser to end your session and contact your administrator for ePO permissions grant.
    
3.  Request the ePO administrator to grant the required permissions. A new user is created in ePO with a user name which is like the email address used in your IdP application, the authentication type is set to SAML authentication, and no permission sets are assigned. An administrator must log on to the ePO console and assign the required permissions to the newly created (IdP) user.
    

**Importing the Root Certificate**

ePO uses SSL for communication between the console and the Tomcat web server, so a certificate is required. When you log on, you are prompted to accept a security certificate.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FKbwPLxj2KmLKF7IbCMYS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D878e6cb8-14b3-4d65-9eaa-002fa687d907&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef7d78cc&sv=2)

1.  Log on to the ePO server. The Certificate Error page appears.
    
2.  Click **Continue to this website**.
    
3.  Click **Certificate Error**.
    
4.  Click **View Certificates**.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fa1z5VbvgvyxJIWb2oz9J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08a4d597-ff02-4ff6-8385-afb1bf1e648b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1c4ff6e&sv=2)

1.  Click **Certification Path** tab.
    
2.  Select the **Orion\_CA\_Name\_of\_Server** certificate and then click **View Certificate**.
    
3.  Click **Install Certificate**.
    
4.  Browse and select **Local Computer** as the physical **store**.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#viewing-editing-port-assignments)

**Viewing/Editing Port Assignments**

Use this page (**Menu** > **Configuration** \> **Settings**) to review and change selected port assignments for communication between the server, the agent, and other components. Click on the information (i) icons for more detailed information regarding each port.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FzIHpd1aw8vVVfpGlVvqX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f2d31db-0078-43d1-a08b-4077a205dc8b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdc26a27&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FI0RV6AERnB3D4ds8tHxx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d6ccdbc-f545-4d82-a533-c08dbc7e2a8f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65314b79&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FuU98c1AUbyrFUVNBbZR6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd8c5b5d-36d4-4ca4-8c31-f26e8317bd83&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec008161&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FrD7DKMDgDh5DmXDtKgVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddca72e51-858a-424c-b259-9023dd944255&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f81820&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FypvhOxZBta5k0jscZvvx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ec73b51-d56f-4422-8448-8c4cfd3b0dd8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83da582a&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FsVMTtFGhdpvsbkq3cpaX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d2c4afb-4981-4826-8085-e99a9ef5debb&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb77ee43&sv=2)

**The Pre-Installation Auditor tool is embedded into the ePO installer by default and identifies port conflicts prior to the installation.**

The figure below shows which ports you can change from this screen. Changes take up to one minute to take effect.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FHvogJzRFecyZoXPmlO3U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98151fe7-dbcf-4ff4-89bb-e12542c657ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb817b16&sv=2)

**IMPORTANT**: Disabling the Agent-server communication secure port is **NOT** recommended as this breaks the agent-to-server communication until the agents are re-installed. Additionally, upon reinstallation, agents are forced to use a less secure, non-TLS communication path to ePO. For information about changing ports, see these Technical Articles:

*   [**KB72936**(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB72936)
    : How to change ePO Agent-to-Server Communication secure port
    
*   [**KB52141**(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB52141)
    : How to change the ePolicy Orchestrator Console-to-Application Server communication port
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#configuring-epo-for-multiple-nics)

**Configuring ePO for Multiple NICs**

If the ePO server is multihomed (has multiple IP addresses), it is recommended to force the server to be bound to the correct interface. The server IP address is used by the master repository and for agent-server communication. If this address is not provided, the IP address of the first NIC in the binding order is used.

1.  Open **C:\\Program Files (X86)\\McAfee\\ePolicy Orchestrator\\DB\\server.ini**.
    
2.  Modify the \[server\] section of the file by adding this line:
    
    1.  **ServerIPaddress=<IP address of server you want ePO to use>**
        
    2.  Example: **ServerIPaddress=192.168.1.203**
        
    
3.  Save and close the server.ini file.
    
4.  Restart all ePO services.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/installation-and-upgrade/post-installation-tasks#basic-installation-troubleshooting)

**Basic Installation Troubleshooting**

Should you have problems with your install, use this methodology to help identify the cause.

*   Ensure minimum installation requirements are met.
    
*   Review Release Notes.
    
*   Review relevant Technical Articles.
    
*   Verify account and permissions.
    
*   Collect exact text of all messages.
    
*   Write down any message codes.
    
*   Review any installer log files (%temp%\\McafeeLogs\\).

# Extension and Package Management | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#installing-and-updating-extensions-manually)

**Installing and Updating Extensions Manually**

If you previously downloaded product components (for example, for ePO extensions), you can install or update them manually. This is a two-step process:

*   Install extensions
    
*   Check in deployment packages
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FCrflJrfEFH5bpjsDg4Bb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2bb491c4-0c35-4283-83b3-6cc455fd2fef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8cd5ee68&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Software**_ \> _**Extensions**_

* * *

Extension files for products or components are in a zip file. To install an extension manually, complete these steps from the ePO console:

1.  Select **Menu** \> **Software** > **Extensions** to open the Extensions page.
    
2.  In the top left corner, click **Install Extension**. The Install Extension dialog box appears.
    
3.  Click **Browse** and browse to and select the desired extension (ZIP) file. Place the extension file in a location that is accessible to the client browser.
    
4.  Click **OK**.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#verifying-installed-updated-extensions)

**Verifying Installed/Updated Extensions**

After the installation is complete, verify the product name appears in the Extensions list in the left page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FrcbQC9OLxgufLlPY_ChRNpU1NpPbkLfHE.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=babc0784&sv=2)

Select (highlight) the extension name in the left page (Example: Endpoint Security) to see information about it in the right pane.

This information includes:

*   **Name**: Lists the name of the extension.
    
*   **Version**: Specifies the version of the currently selected extension. **Note**: Multiple versions of the same extension can be installed.
    
*   **Installed by**: Specifies the user who installed the currently selected extension.
    
*   **Status**: Identifies whether the extension was installed successfully. If it was not installed successfully, any errors are identified.
    
*   **Requires**: Specifies any extensions that the currently selected extension depends on.
    
*   **Details**: Lists details of extension installation.
    
*   **Modules**: Specifies the modules that are controlled by this extension and whether they are running. This is valuable for troubleshooting.
    
*   **Remove**: Removes the selected extension from the Extensions list.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#removing-extensions-manually)

**Removing Extensions Manually**

Click on each number below to see the process for manually removing extensions.

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#card-title-12)
> 
> Adding and Updating Packages Manually
> 
> The ePO Main Repository is physically located on the ePO server in the ePO software installation directory (\\DB\\Software). It is always the primary repository for the ePO environment. As part of the deployment, you must check the package into the ePO Main Repository.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FydSmHUVFgufESm2PMomc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b96ba1c-501c-44e9-a7d5-be768a097199&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcdd0888&sv=2)

From the Menu page, select **Software** \> **Main Repository**.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#card-title-14)

Step 2 Title

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FHbPyGfQ10QXEjFOKZ9IW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6d8c90c-b6aa-464b-8df0-9369c13ffc7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7476d8df&sv=2)

Click **Check In Package**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FZtHMb3GLVd7bNhItp0G4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df371dcb8-ab95-4313-bae5-acce17dc74b7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9afc65f&sv=2)

*   For Package type, make sure Product or Update (.ZIP) is selected.
    
*   Click **Browse.**
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fd03ui7sbnBemdxk6MTvc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5eeca30c-5bc5-4d7b-9a69-a6d42fba1f9a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=18711c34&sv=2)

*   Navigate to the zipped packed path and select the .ZIP package file. Do not unzip the package.
    
*   Click **Open**.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FyJcItzqklDLvzQB92fc7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d2fbbd5-0f54-4a6e-b55d-0585b1e479bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbeedfac&sv=2)

On the **Check In Package** dialog, make sure the selected package displays in the text box and then click **Next**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FVfSQWqpkt7YUkbG2Hs96%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eb1f84b-614c-4be4-b488-cc0ef2878aeb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69885917&sv=2)

*   Review the information about the package, including Name, Version, Type, and Language.
    
*   For Branch, make sure **Current** is selected.
    
*   Notice the package is signed.
    
*   Click **Save**.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#card-title-19)

Summary

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F294tCCZuGYnIGKsFbGP0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ed8915-bb18-4386-aef9-1ac03a889651&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e821299&sv=2)

*   Wait while the package is adding to the Main Repository. You are returned to the Main Repository after the process is complete.
    
*   Locate the product in the list. Review key information, such as _Status_, _Type_, _Version_, _Minor Version_, _Check-In Date_, and _Branch_.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/extension-and-package-management#removing-packages-manually)

**Removing Packages Manually**

To manually remove a software package from the ePO console, do the following:

1.  Click **Menu** \> **Software** \> **Main Repository**.
    
2.  Select the package you want to remove.
    
3.  Expand the **Actions** entry at the bottom.
    
4.  Click **Delete Package**.
    
5.  On the _Delete Package_ confirmation screen, verify the package information to remove and click **OK**.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FG40Km3vGlJFibIpM_D5bwYTTqHixdc7HZ.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d794d0e0&sv=2)

**Check the Audit Log (**_**Menu > Reporting > Audit Log**_**) to verify removal of extensions and packages.**

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   ePO simplifies the process of deploying products to the managed systems in your network by providing a user interface to configure and schedule deployments.
    
*   From the Software Catalog, you can download, check in, update, and remove managed product components from your server.
    
*   There are two processes you can follow to deploy products using ePO: product deployment projects and client tasks.
    
*   Client tasks automate system management activities, such as product deployment, upgrades, and updates.
    
*   Client tasks can be assigned at any level in the System Tree and are inherited by groups and systems lower in the tree. As with policies and policy assignments, you can break the inheritance for an assigned client task.
    
*   You can export and import client tasks for use with other ePO servers.
    
*   The Client Task Catalog is used to add and manage client tasks.
    
*   The Client Task Comparison tool is used to compare client tasks that are similar, allowing you to determine which settings are different and which are the same.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/module-summary#in-the-next-lesson-you-will-learn-how-to-manage-policies-in-epo)

In the next lesson, you will learn how to manage policies in ePO.

[PreviousCreating a Custom Properties Client Task Simulation](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/creating-a-custom-properties-client-task-simulation)
[NextModule Intro](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/policy-management/module-intro)

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   User accounts allow you to control how people access and use ePO.
    
*   While user account and permission sets are closely related, they are created and configured using separate steps.
    
*   ePO contains default permission sets to assign or use as templates.
    
*   For quick migration, define permission sets and then export and import them to other servers.
    

In the next lesson, you will learn about ePO Dashboards, queries, and reports.

[PreviousCreating a New Permission Set Simulation](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/creating-a-new-permission-set-simulation)
[NextModule Intro](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/module-intro)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

User accounts allow you to control how people access and use ePO. While user accounts and permission sets are closely related, they are created and configured using separate steps.

In this module, you will learn about the default permission sets that ePO provides, guidelines on using permission sets, and how to create, customize, and manage permission sets. You will also learn how to create and manage user accounts, the different options for account authentication, and ways to automate user account management, such as using Active Directory.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Define user accounts and permission sets
    
*   Configure settings for users and permission sets
    
*   Edit, disable, and delete user accounts
    
*   Edit and export permission sets
    
*   Create users and assign permission sets
    

[PreviousModule Summary](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/policy-management/module-summary)
[NextUser Accounts](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/user-accounts)

Last updated 1 year ago

# ePServer Configuration | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#server-settings)

**Server Settings**

All the necessary settings specific to your ePO server are in Server Settings. The available entries here allow you to fine-tune you ePO server based on the needs of your organization. Customizations made here affect all your ePO users.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FuX1BxRgBvhjwo6N0XGO6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc7a39af-6e4c-4cfe-b0a3-6782cdc1b959&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84da4f35&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Configuration**_ \> _**Server Settings**_

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#password-policy)

**Password Policy**

The ePO 5.10 release added the Password Policy feature, which allows you to define the strength of a password. For example, an administrator can restrict the number of previously used passwords and limit the number of days before the password expires.

To use this feature, administrators must manually enable these settings via the Password Policy setting category in Server Settings as this feature is not enabled by default.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FdyXBCSqDUh1ePAropOI8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06f955d5-3ecd-466e-806f-a9a4ebe3c4c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=facff91&sv=2)

Select the **Password Policy** Setting Category, then click **Edit**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fndw5U4vEMt8zEbTUUK7b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da96612cb-017e-4848-bb5d-ac57daea8a70&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5411de2a&sv=2)

Once enabled, available options for this feature include:

*   Password Strength **Criteria**: Passwords can be defined as having 7-30 characters, and must contain at least one of the following characters:
    
    *   Uppercase
        
    *   Lowercase
        
    *   Numeric
        
    *   Special
        
    
*   **Password Expiration Criteria**: Expiration dates from 30-365 days can be configured before a password expires
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#logon-protection)

**Logon Protection**

The ePO 5.10 release also added the ability to set user account lockouts based on multiple logon attempts or restrict access via IP address management thru the Logon Protection server setting.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FtKzl6h8NTpD9diOcSeJm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D331efce6-c944-4bca-83b7-23393cd34339&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1393b20&sv=2)

*   Select the **Logon Protection** Setting Category, then click **Edit.**
    
*   Click on the **Automatic Responses** link under **Notifications** to create you own customizable default response to failed logon attempts.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F7itC6rbR1U92FH2jrMVg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4c3d2c5-67cb-4252-a8d2-d93bf1fa2b87&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f555ab7&sv=2)

Enable these features to provide added logon protection:

*   **Lock Out User Accounts**: Enable this feature to lock out a user account after the configurable failed attempts is met.
    
*   **Restrict IP Addresses**: Enable this feature to automatically block an IP address if 10 or more failed attempts occur in under 60 seconds.
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#queries-page)

**Queries Page**

**Queries** is a new category introduced in the Server settings page. Use the Queries page to set the maximum number of elements that display in the following chart types:

*   Single-Line Chart
    
*   Bar Chart
    
*   Stacked Bar Chart
    
*   Single Group Summary Table
    
*   Bubble Chart
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FvjvWCGcz9rMSJCquDmzq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbcf4081-24a0-47b7-82ba-7bef1601c247&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21fdcff6&sv=2)

**Higher number of elements may affect query and chart performance. You can set the maximum limit up to 2000 for any of the chart types.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#email-encryption)

**Email Encryption**

**Email Encryption (TLS support)** is a new setting on the **Email Server** page in the Server Settings.

*   Provides the secure channel (SMTP over TLS) for email support in ePO
    
*   Allows you to enable/disable the TLS support
    
*   When you enable this option, the port number in **SMTP server port** updates from an existing port number to 587
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FhTfqZdTGkEbYM6meNW3m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fa433df-7bc2-48fa-a7a6-fd1a9f0eb732&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4ac16d&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#server-information)

**Server Information**

The Server Information Settings page specifies Java, OpenSSL, and Apache server information for the ePO and database server, such as name, IP address, and version information. You can export the Server Information page details to a CSV file.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FlnQc9K2ljNh0Q4r5eQjF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97a0c120-1696-4778-934e-56e600254e5f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f64da6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#personal-settings)

**Personal Settings**

**Personal Settings** in the ePO console allows you to customize the ePO server to your environmental needs.

To configure Personal Settings, go to **Menu** \> **Configuration** \> **Personal Settings**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FA28HmHchxrmGN415vGSD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54fbc6fa-5fc2-4449-92e0-c2cbcd0893c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2af4f9a&sv=2)

In **Personal Settings**, you can modify items such as:

*   **Appearance**: Provides the ability to change the display color of a selected entry in the console
    
*   **Password**: This option is no longer available from within Personal Settings; see the “Change Password” entry under the Help icon on the banner bar
    
*   **Queries and Reports Warning**: Determines whether a warning message appears when you try to drag a query from one query group to another
    
*   **System Tree Settings**: Determines whether a warning message appears when you try to drag systems or groups from one System Tree group to another. Enable auto-expand (default) of System Tree nodes when moving one system to another.
    
*   **Tables**: Identifies how often auto-refreshed tables are refreshed during your session
    
*   **Time Zone Preference**: Provides the ability to set the desired time zone for your ePO server
    
*   **User Session**: Controls the length of time that your user session remains open after you stop interacting with the user interface
    

* * *

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#registered-servers)

**Registered Servers**

Various types of additional servers in a customer environment can be registered in the ePO server, allowing you to integrate ePO with other external servers. To configure these external servers, go to **Menu** \> **Configuration** \> **Registered Servers**.

**Registered servers are servers that work with your ePO server to support or add functionality. When you install ePO for the first time, no other servers are registered with your ePO server.**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FHZKZYG87XsdDK23QHDcO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3e56da7-7238-4872-96a8-22b8f1d91958&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=437575e8&sv=2)

Click **New Server** to create a new registered server, or click **Action** to delete or edit an existing registered server. You can register several types of servers with your main ePO server, including:

*   **LDAP servers**: Registering this type of server allows you to use Policy Assignment rules to dynamically enable assigned permission sets and to enable Active Directory (AD) User Login; Active Directory servers are an example of LDAP servers that can be used to synchronize and import systems from an AD server to the ePO System Tree.
    
*   **Other ePO servers**: Registering this type of server allows you to collect or aggregate data or transfer managed systems between the registered servers.
    
*   **SNMP servers**: Registering this type of server allows ePO to know where to send the trap to so it can receive the trap info.
    
*   **Syslog servers**: Registering this type of server allows ePO to forward events received from clients to the syslog server.
    
*   **Additional, remote, database servers**: Registering this type of server allows you to retrieve data from the database in queries, reports, dashboard monitors, and server tasks.
    

* * *

**See the** [_**Registered Servers**_(opens in a new tab)](https://docs.trellix.com/bundle/epolicy-orchestrator-5.10.0-product-guide/page/GUID-946575D1-FA11-4B1A-B872-5DC6FDE8AA2C.html)
 **section in the ePO 5.10 Product Guide for additional details on registering servers in ePO.**

* * *

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#agent-handlers)

**Agent Handlers**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#what-are-agent-handlers)

**What are Agent Handlers?**

Agent Handlers are an ePO server component that handle communication between Agent and an ePO server. Each installation of ePO includes an Agent Handler. Agent Handlers can be deployed independently on systems throughout your network. These servers should be on the same network as the ePO server and not on a remote network across a WAN link.

*   By default, the ePO server acts as an Agent Handler.
    
*   Agent Handlers helps offload the demand on the ePO server.
    
*   They can help scale the ePO infrastructure and reduce the load on the ePO server.
    
*   They can take care of all the ASCI communication.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#how-agent-handlers-work)

**How Agent Handlers Work**

Managed system is assigned to Agent Handler[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#managed-system-is-assigned-to-agent-handler)

Agent Handlers distribute network traffic, which is generated by an agent-to-server communication interval (ASCI), by assigning managed systems or groups of systems to report to a specific Agent Handler. You can assign single system or groups of systems, as well as have distinct groups assigned to different Agent Handlers.

System performs regular ASCI[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#system-performs-regular-asci)

After assignment, a managed system performs regular agent-server communication to its Agent Handler instead of to the main ePO server. Like the ePO server, communications between agents and Agent Handlers are over an Industry‑standard Transport Layer Security (TLS) network protocol for secure network transmissions.

Agent pulls necessary files and information from its Agent Handler[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#agent-pulls-necessary-files-and-information-from-its-agent-handler)

The Agent Handler provides updated sitelists, policies, and policy assignment rules to clients. The handler also supplies repository content to clients configured to update from the master repository. The agent handler on the ePO server provides the content directly; additional agent handlers cache files from the main repository as clients request them. When an agent requests content from its handler, if the handler does not have the files needed, the handler retrieves them from the Main Repository and passes them to the agent. The files are cached on the additional agent handler so that subsequent requests for the same file do not require additional traffic from the Main Repository.

Repositories[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#repositories)

*   By default, requested repository files are cached in C:\\Program Files (x86)\\McAfee\\ePolicy Orchestrator\\DB\\RepoCache directory on the ePO server or remote Agent Handler.
    
*   The primary ePO server (i.e., the system that has the ePO Application Server service installed) hosts the Main Repository.
    
*   Agent Handlers transparently handle requests for software and cache the required files after downloading from the main repository.
    
*   No configuration is necessary.
    

Data Channel[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#data-channel)

*   API extension for Trellix products integration
    
*   Mechanism for Trellix products to exchange messages between their endpoint plugins and their management extensions
    
*   Agent properties, tagging, and policy computation performed directly against database
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#logical-epo-infrastructure)

**Logical ePO Infrastructure**

An Agent Handler is installed as a part of the primary ePO server. This is sufficient for many small ePO installations. For larger and more complex networks, you can distribute services across the network by installing additional Agent Handlers.

*   These additional Agent Handlers co-exist within a single logical ePO infrastructure.
    
*   You can deploy Agent Handlers on separate hardware or virtual machines that coexist within a single logical ePO infrastructure.
    
*   An Agent Handler installation includes only the Trellix ePO Server service (Apache Server) and Trellix ePO Event Parser service.
    
    *   The Trellix ePO Server service communicates with the Trellix Agent, receives updated events and properties from the agents, and sends updated policies and tasks as assigned by administrators in the ePO console.
        
    *   The Trellix ePO Event Parser service receives events from the Trellix ePO Server service, which in turn receives them from the clients.
        
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FYjOi6vfFkhIY1TAjQJyq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0c71c3f-776f-45d7-a6eb-cc26612fbb43&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6c23da5&sv=2)

**Agent Handler Requirements**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FmIGepr7svvdldyAze9uI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df958fa59-f01c-4c64-a748-c8be2e4a4219&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a7f4c87&sv=2)

Agent Handlers can be installed on virtual infrastructure systems, such as VMware ESX.

Their hardware and software requirements and CPU load are approximately the same as an ePO server.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#important-notes)

**Important Notes**

*   Agent Handlers (AH) are NOT a solution to low bandwidth.
    
*   An additional Agent Handler with low bandwidth to the SQL server has WORSE performance than just having agents connect to the ePO server.
    
*   A single Agent Handler with a poor connection to SQL will have a massive performance impact on the whole ePO infrastructure, not just the clients it is handling.
    
    *   When one AH is interacting with the database, the other AHs are locked out. The AH with the poor connection locks the database for large amounts of time, preventing the other AHs from working.
        
    
*   Agent Handlers MUST have a high-speed connection to the SQL server and a stable connection to the SQL server database.
    
*   If the database serving the ePO server is under heavy load, adding Agent Handlers will not help.
    
*   You may need to upgrade your SQL server hardware to take advantage of multiple Agent Handlers.
    
*   Agent Handlers should be co-located with the SQL server and never installed in “remote” locations.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#required-ports)

**Required Ports**

Installing the Agent Handler server hardware, software, and configuring the firewall ports are the first steps before using ePO to manage systems behind a DMZ.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FECt5APEzN4dPyFbsVGsy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2490654e-c4f9-4ddc-ab77-31458cd797fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec76e69d&sv=2)

1.  Build the Agent Handler server hardware with the Microsoft Windows server Operating System.
    
2.  In the DMZ of your firewall protected network, install the Agent Handler server hardware and Microsoft Windows server operating system.
    
3.  Configure your Domain Name System (DNS) server to host the Agent Handler server to the internal ePO network.
    
4.  Configure these ports on the _internal-facing_ firewall to communicate between the ePO server and the Agent Handler in DMZ:
    
    1.  **Port 80** — Bidirectional
        
    2.  **Port 8443** — Bidirectional
        
    3.  **Port 8444** — Bidirectional
        
    4.  **Port 443** — Bidirectional
        
    
5.  **Optional**: If your SQL database is installed on a different server than your ePO server, configure these two ports on the _internal-facing_ firewall to connect to the Agent Handler:
    
    1.  **Port 1433 TCP** — Bidirectional
        
    2.  **Port 1434 UDP** — Bidirectional
        
    
6.  Configure these ports on the _public-facing_ firewall to communicate between the ePO server and the Agent Handler in the DMZ:
    
    1.  **Port 80 TCP** — Inbound
        
    2.  **Port 443 TCP** — Inbound
        
    3.  **Port 8081 TCP** — Inbound
        
    4.  **Port 8082 UDP** — Inbound
        
    

Now you have installed your Agent Handler hardware and server operating system in the DMZ. Plus, you configured all ports to connect through the firewall, between the ePO server and database to the Agent Handler server.

**See** [**KB66797**(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB66797)
 **for additional information regarding ePO port requirements for firewall traffic.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#agent-handler-deployment)

**Agent Handler Deployment**

The figure below shows the workflow for an Agent Handler deployment.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FjLt3E10yw9VAh9OKNS7l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D359f7bf1-3418-45e0-8cb5-4b4bc9d6d64e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=615dd871&sv=2)

**Updating the ePO Server and the Agent Handlers**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F2QAeGqQyMQT6K5PJwnNl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd87b9a93-eb0f-4630-89e4-68187d8a10e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52154ca6&sv=2)

**The ePO server and the Agent Handler must be at the same patch level. The Agent Handler checks the database version every 30 seconds and disables itself if a different schema is found.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#configuring-agent-handlers)

**Configuring Agent Handlers**

After the installation is complete, your next step is to set up Agent Handlers in your network and assign Trellix Agents to them. Agent handler management is performed from the Agent Handlers page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FHwOQz4NgJjo20l0WvTon%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a42c6fb-dc88-4b3a-84bb-dcdf54faac0b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f9b6165&sv=2)

**Tasks**

*   Create Agent Handler groups
    
*   Manage Agent Handler groups
    
*   Assign Trellix Agents to Agent Handlers
    
*   Manage Agent Handler assignments
    
*   Move agents between handlers
    

**Agent Handlers Page**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FFi2LXcxUyWKas8S7RCXt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a13cd97-27f9-464e-bca7-f7632c414066&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b23fde4b&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Configuration**_ \> _**Agent Handlers**_

* * *

The Agent Handlers page consists of four monitors:

1.  **Handler Status**: Specifies the number of active and out-of-date handlers
    
2.  **Systems per Agent Handler**: Specifies the number of agents assigned to each Agent Handler
    
3.  **Handler Groups**: Specifies the number of Agent Handler groups that the ePO server manages
    
4.  **Handler Assignment Rules**: Displays the list of Agent Handler assignments in your environment, their priority, and details about rule settings
    

Click the active areas in each monitor to drill down and view more details about the systems informing each monitor.

Actions within the Agent Handler Confirmation page are: **At the top of the page:**

*   **New Assignment**: Opens the Agent Handler Assignment page. Use this to create a new Agent Handler Assignment
    
*   **Edit Priority**: Opens the Edit Priority page. Use this page to change priority of the Agent Handler Assignments
    

**By using the Actions Button in the Handler Assignment Rules window:**

*   **Import**: Imports a previously exported Agent Handler Assignment list
    
*   **Export**: Opens the Download Agent Handler Assignment page. Use this to download an xml file containing the Agent Handler Assignment list
    

**Handler Assignment Rules: Row Actions**: Specifies the actions you can perform on selected Agent Handler assignments, including:

*   **To Edit**: Click the blue hyperlink Assignment name to open the Edit Assignment page. Use this to edit the settings of the selected Agent Handler Assignment
    
*   **Delete**: Deletes the selected agent
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#certificate-manager)

**Certificate Manager**

As discussed in the previous lesson, the Certificate Manager is another part of the basic server configuration. The latest certificates are loaded by default with a fresh installation of ePO, but if you have upgraded from an older version of ePO, ensure you migrate the ePO certificates to the latest hash algorithm.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FuRqTzb7Qw61slIeIjmur%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D369e1b45-3562-482e-889c-ce85a1e750d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed85e2d0&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Configuration**_ \> _**Certificate Manager**_

* * *

The Certificate Manager allows you to:

*   Migrate certificates that are signed by older signing algorithm to the new algorithm such as SHA-1 to SHA-256
    
*   Regenerate your certificates when your existing certificates are compromised due to vulnerabilities in your environment
    
*   Migrate or regenerate certificates for managed products that are derived from ePO root CA
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/epserver-configuration#registered-executables)

**Registered Executables**

The registered executables you configure are run when the conditions of a rule are met. Automatic Responses trigger the registered executable command to run.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FgQvjwFIsMJiwi5pgaK1Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92311ecb-ddf1-45ff-a8d5-4596c295e41a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=420c67b&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Configuration**_ \> _**Registered Executables**_

* * *

*   **You can only run registered executable commands on console applications.**
    
*   **You must be on the local server system when adding or editing a registered executable in the ePO console.**

# Duplicating and Editing a Policy Simulation | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

Welcome to the Duplicating and Editing a Policy simulation.

In this simulation, you will create a custom policy for Trellix Agent. The Default General policy meets most of your needs, so you will duplicate and edit it to fit your specific requirements.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FWNgcvUVcbW7yhLPPMOMp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18291d50-f9b2-4e5d-a34e-cea98684cd69&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97b833de&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FnAOS908UQ4QlOyKbEIg7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd26f7125-0c16-40c0-84b5-f7084a951fb4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3dc9f37d&sv=2)

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

After ePO is deployed, it is important to monitor your network’s security status on an ongoing basis. Keeping constant watch on your environment is a difficult task. Dashboards help you do this. ePO comes with its own querying and reporting capabilities, which are customizable, flexible, and easy to use.

In this module, you will learn the about the types of dashboards included with ePO that you can use immediately, how to create and customize dashboards, and recommendations for designing dashboards. You will learn how permissions control dashboard access and use and factors that impact dashboard load time. You will also learn how to use queries and reports to gather information about activities that occur on your ePO server and throughout your network.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Identify the purpose of dashboards and monitors, as well as features and capabilities
    
*   Identify default dashboards included with ePO
    
*   Add and duplicate a dashboard
    
*   Edit and assign dashboard permissions
    
*   Query the ePO database
    
*   Use the Query Builder to create your own queries
    
*   Configure query permissions
    
*   Export query data to view outside of ePO
    
*   Identify the report management process
    

[PreviousModule Summary](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/module-summary)
[NextePO Dashboards](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/epo-dashboards)

Last updated 1 year ago

# User Accounts | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/user-accounts#overview)

**Overview**

User accounts are another important user management feature and provide a means for users to access and use the ePO console. Each user account is associated with one or more permissions sets which determine rights and access to ePO.

There are two types of users:

*   Administrators with permissions to all products and features
    
*   Users with defined access based upon the permission set their account is assigned to
    

![Menu &gt; Users Management &gt; Users](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fspf-Rk7KgUuwNVd0_dq3NMaaQwnmXX8K9.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b17dd39&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Users Management**_ > _**Users**_

The figure below shows the User page.

_**Click on the information (i) icons for detailed information on each field.**_

To edit a user account:
