# System Tree | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

The System Tree is one of the most important pieces of your managed environment. It is the logical representation of your managed environment. Your System Tree dictates:

*   How your policies for different products are inherited
    
*   How your client tasks are inherited
    
*   What groups your systems go into
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#system-tree-overview)

**System Tree Overview**

The ePO server is responsible for managing exactly one System Tree. The System Tree contains all of the systems that ePO manages. A system is a managed machine, a server, workstation, laptop or an appliance. Within the System Tree, each system is represented by its NetBIOS name. Internally to ePO, each system is represented by its Globally Unique Identifier (GUID).

You can open the page two ways:

*   Click the **System Tree** category on the navigation bar
    
*   Select **Menu** \> **Systems** \> **System Tree**
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FnW66ieIMuCagEiPM8rvg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78edb070-0cd0-4365-a508-060836ae7b04&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d767762&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#hierarchical-structure)

**Hierarchical Structure**

The System Tree initially contains two containers (groups), but lets you create additional groups to meet your organizational needs. These groups display in the tree in a hierarchical manner.

*   **My Organization**: Top-level (root) group. **It cannot be renamed or deleted**. All systems are organized within it in logical containers called groups and subgroups.
    
*   **Lost and Found**: Default subgroup where systems with unknown locations are placed. It always appears last in the list and is not alphabetized among its peers. It cannot be renamed or deleted.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FJnDvPQOqugHY7HE8q2kX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2174867d-632d-4fe4-b432-e62944a72bb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b22e645&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#groups)

**Groups**

Although you can add all systems into one group in the System Tree, a flat list makes setting different policies for different systems very difficult, especially for large networks. By grouping systems, you can manage their policies in one place, rather than individually. You also can schedule system tasks (such as update of virus definition files) at any level of the System Tree, as well as sort systems by IP address or tags.

You can group systems based on:

*   Machine-type: Laptops, servers, or desktops
    
*   Geography: North America or Europe
    
*   Political Boundaries (Organization Departments): Finance or Development
    
*   Any other logical criteria that supports your needs
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FsRg7qzcIw6PVhPjfjfSo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2aea9c7a-0b20-445a-9c0a-df58822c2345&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48afe2a8&sv=2)

**As a best practice, create only as much structure as is useful for the functionality of your ePO environment.**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#building-the-system-tree)

**Building the System Tree**

During this process, you create the groups to hold your managed systems and then add your systems to the appropriate groups. The groups you add are always subgroups within the top-level My Organization group.

There’s no single way to build your System Tree. Because every network is different, your System Tree organization can be as unique as your network layout. You can use more than one method to build and organize the System Tree, as shown in the figure below.

**Inheritance**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F3v7qrk9FQhmfCAOPg6yY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d3dee27-bedb-4f26-8250-cff4481fc44d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53953620&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FxkXuiDeOFjaGADMSq1up%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71cfad4f-9c61-4849-a60b-0a5445724adf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7755e2fa&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#adding-groups-subgroups-and-systems-manually)

**Adding Groups/Subgroups and Systems Manually**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#adding-groups-manually)

**Adding Groups Manually**

The manual build process is useful where no formal Microsoft environment exists (Example: using a NetWare-based network) or when the Microsoft Networking environment does not map well to the anti-virus management structure that you require.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FM39WoyWWwKY0cS17g8DR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03c80a61-f6ee-4841-b2ca-b36b117f7938&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88f90a43&sv=2)

1.  From the **System Tree**, select a parent group. If this is the first group, the parent is **My Organization**.
    
2.  Click the **New Subgroups** box at the top of the page, or select **System Tree Actions** > **New Subgroups**.
    
3.  In the **Name** box, enter the group name, and click **OK**. If adding multiple groups, separate the names with a comma.
    
4.  The new group appears in the System Tree. Repeat as necessary until you are ready to populate the groups with the desired systems.
    

**After you add a system, note it initially has an** _**Unmanaged State**_**. You must wake up agents on the systems to change the status to** _**Managed**_**. The Agent Wakeup process is discussed in more detail later in the course**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FQsHs6hNYZ3y5COiMLOic%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4775dfdd-3b1f-4150-a458-a77452d25b04&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f34ce047&sv=2)

Whatever group is highlighted is the one the action will be applied to, so when selecting New Subgroups the new groups will appear under the highlighted group.

* * *

**When adding more than one group at a time, the groups should be separated by commas.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#adding-systems-manually)

**Adding Systems Manually**

To add systems manually, click on the **New Systems** button on the System Tree page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F1AhAf86RLSrDIKaLCC0j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D704b316e-fa8a-4803-8b05-295a508178dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7aa9cf1b&sv=2)

*   In this example, the systems are added and the Trellix Agent is pushed at this time.
    
*   The systems will shows as Unmanaged in the System Tree until the agent is installed and has reported back to ePO that the installation is complete.
    

* * *

From the **New Systems** page in the **How to add systems** section, select one of these options. **Note**: The fields on the page vary, depending on your selection.

*   **Push agents and add systems to the current group**: Adds systems and deploys agent
    
*   **Push agents and place systems in the System Tree according to sorting criteria**: Deploys agents to the specified systems in the groups of the System Tree, according to sorting criteria
    
*   **Add systems to the current group (TechLearn), but do not push agents**: Adds systems but does not deploy agent
    
*   **Create and download agent installation package**: Creates a custom agent installation package in which you can embed credentials for the installation. The package can be distributed to managed node users for self-install. The package (FramePkg.exe or install.sh) is created when you install ePO or check in an agent package. **Note**: Node users require administrative privileges to install the agent.
    
*   **Import systems from a text file into the selected group, but do not deploy agents**: Imports systems from a properly generated text file but does not deploy agents to these systems
    
*   **Create URL for client-side agent download**: The administrator can create and distribute a custom agent URL to managed node users for self-install. Each user copies and pastes the URL into a browser. The user is directed to a specific site to download an installation package, then uses the Smart Installer to install the agent.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#importing-system-tree-structure)

**Importing System Tree Structure**

Another way to manually build the System Tree is with the **Import Tree Structure** function on the **System Tree** > **Group Details** tab. Using this function, you import a text file saved to a temporary directory on the ePO server.

You can add systems to existing groups or subgroups, as well add new groups, subgroups, and/or systems. Systems added to the System Tree have an unmanaged state until after an agent wakeup.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FgiAWSCA84Urmw3oY6GNW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4089ede-90de-40ac-8980-fc1490f1d98d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1fad046&sv=2)

*   From the **Group Details** tab in the System Tree, select **Actions** \> **Import Tree Structure**.
    
*   Import a text file from a temporary directory on the server.
    

**Note**: The text file must use UTF-8 file encoding to correctly import system names with double-byte or extended characters in them. There are third-party utilities available that can export a list of your computers into a text file. Windows 2000 and above provides CSVDE.EXE and LDIFDE.EXE, that you can use to export Active Directory objects, such as computers.

* * *

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#moving-groups-and-systems)

**Moving Groups and Systems**

After you populate your system tree, you can move the existing groups/subgroups and systems.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fr6CvBHranytjpmDTlCBh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5633c1ec-aecd-49ec-8dd5-a79965cd295b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c9d4bec&sv=2)

1.  Locate the system in the System Tree.
    
2.  Mark the checkbox for the system.
    
3.  Select **Directory Management** \> **Move Systems**. A page displays a list that resembles your tree structure.
    
4.  Select the new group or subgroup for the system.
    
5.  Click **OK**.
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#customized-option-for-system-tree-groups-expand-and-collapse)

**Customized Option for System Tree Groups Expand and Collapse**

*   Allows Enable/Disable for auto expanding of System Tree groups
    
*   New option to support System Tree structure customization (only when moving one system to another system)
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FDEqG8dOnsJ0cidkyGxzP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D897888bf-8377-4353-babf-e849ad33fb49&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=372257e2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#nt-domain-synchronization)

**NT Domain Synchronization**

This feature lets you populate your System Tree automatically by synchronizing entire NT domains with specified groups. This approach is an easy way to add all systems in your network to the System Tree simultaneously. The systems are imported as a flat list with no system descriptions.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#nt-domain-synchronization-overview)

**NT Domain Synchronization Overview**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FZOv2QzPeSkDbJHIUy9lP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f29f324-25ba-4ace-b5e2-2b1486e26221&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d1d8668&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#synchronizing-nt-domains)

**Synchronizing NT Domains**

If you are using containers within your ePO Directory, that correspond exactly with the name of domains or workgroups with your browse list, you can use the Synchronize Domains task to add and delete systems, manually or automatically, to or from these groups.

You can only synchronize the contents of domains or workgroups, within the browse list, with groups of the same name. If the domains or workgroups selected during task creation do not exist in the ePO System Tree, they are automatically added as groups.

If there is an existing group with the same name as a domain or workgroups you select, the computers in the domain are added to that group. In addition to placing the system into the ePO Directory, the Synchronize Domains task will install the Trellix Agents.

_**Click on the information (i) icons for detailed information on each field.**_

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FGa7EhN5mXK7gnAj6Ab7V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1ce5e24-28bb-48c5-8b60-37c813a96e4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c7a8288&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FayCLIHWljubyzs4TIQ80%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22cb08de-16f3-4302-9ffb-2bbb02f5fe5e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=515f5d71&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FXhjSulXOM20Q6l7EBzFd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1a480ca-0ad3-4e72-89e5-78e32617bcf0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ace3f1e2&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FsyVkuGL9gH8nFQ0ExZAo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9904e6ef-1b82-47d0-96ce-3dc4b77b74d7&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7615efa5&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FqoSs4lmhiTGnbKpWMpv8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e7fc63b-578b-4869-be37-f944c6b98ed8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8eb0030&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FpgHNCRkDsUDSGvorCwhP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D210c7b0a-8b20-4a44-a749-c70b1f87f493&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6ce2619&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F3UzrQyDRa845g0gnFA3T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bc23dee-afc7-4397-80b4-76006b2867be&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aef6b9f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#configuring-agent-pushing-settings-if-selected)

**Configuring Agent Pushing Settings (if selected)**

If you select **Push agents to new systems when they are discovered**, configure the **Agent Push Settings**. Click the **Configure Settings** button to display the Agent Push Settings page.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FX17EY0cseBycMgnwBNIo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50b13429-772d-46ed-88e5-a92fb1736f6c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adcc76cc&sv=2)

Select the agent version to install, decide which systems to include in the agent push, and determine the path that the agent files will be installed to on the client machine. In addition, you must provide local administrator credentials for installing the agent. Set the number of installation attempts desired, as well as the retry interval.

*   **Installation options**: Specifies the agent installation options available, including:
    
    *   **Install only on systems that do not have an agent**: Sends the agent installation package only to systems without an agent installed. When deselected, sends the agent installation package to all selected systems, regardless of whether the agent is already installed on them.
        
    *   **Force installation over existing version**: Replaces existing agents within the selected group with the selected versions. This option is not available when you select Install only on systems that do not have an agent.
        
    
*   **Push Agent Using**: Select the connection used for the deployment as either:
    
    *   **Selected Agent Handler**: Select the server from the list.
        
    *   **All Agent Handlers**: Use all handers.
        
    

_**This feature applies to the Active Directory and NT Domain Synchronization features.**_

* * *

**It is recommended that you do not deploy the agent during the initial import if the domain is large. Deploying the Trellix Agent package to many systems at once may cause network traffic issues. Instead, import the domain, then deploy the agent to smaller groups of systems at a time, rather than all at once. However, once you have deployed agents, consider revisiting this page and selecting this option after the initial agent deployment, so that the agent is installed automatically on any new systems that are added to the group (or its subgroups) through domain synchronization.**

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#active-directory-synchronization-overview)

**Active Directory Synchronization Overview**

This feature is designed for networks with an existing Active Directory. Like NT Domain Synchronization, it lets you import systems only as a flat list; however, it also lets you import systems and the Active Directory container structure to ensure your System Tree mirrors your Active Directory. It also imports system descriptions.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FzX8YTCLOAM8rMBSBDEvR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc6e1ce9-6fe7-4f67-8e05-74acf6b73ed2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75148b16&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#registering-ldap-server)

**Registering LDAP Server**

A registered LDAP server is required. If your server is not registered, complete this step prior to configuring AD Synchronization.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F3BudF08yw5LgbO6kQYcC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbf3b1e2-0f2d-453b-9252-efc8b99b1065&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=233a304e&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Configuration**_ \> _**Registered Servers**_ \> _**New Server**_

* * *

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#synchronizing-active-directory)

**Synchronizing Active Directory**

If you are using containers within your ePO Directory that correspond exactly with the name of domains or workgroups in your browse list, you can use the Synchronize Domains task to add and delete systems, manually or automatically, to or from these groups.

You can only synchronize the contents of domains or workgroups within the browse list with groups of the same name. If the domains or workgroups selected during task creation do not exist in the ePO System Tree, they are automatically added as groups.

If there is an existing group with the same name as a domain or workgroups you select, the computers in the domain are added to that group. In addition to placing the system into the ePO Directory, the Synchronize Domains task will install the agents.

_**Click on the information (i) icons for detailed information on each field.**_

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FB24B1GaCBO6RCH3LCouw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38ffa511-6e98-4df4-a306-df4bb4d58c74&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91c13bf0&sv=2)

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FlF19KK3omSYwUeYbfgJM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1033a57-1786-424a-bea2-83231af78fe2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e7d716d&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/server-configuration/system-tree#maintaining-synchronization)

**Maintaining Synchronization**

After you specify Active Directory Synchronization or NT Domains at the Group level, you can continually maintain the listing of computers contained in the console tree by running an **Active Directory Synchronization/NT Domain** server task or by manually updating the synchronized group. This task synchronizes selected Windows NT domains and Active Directory containers that are mapped to System Tree groups.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FC7WyFaSyxCyvtngfyV4Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc59f489-955b-40ab-84d5-e437ca9a3fe2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95c7173d&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Automation**_ \> _**Server Tasks**_ > _**New Task**_

# Creating a New Permission Set Simulation | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F4MM9wv4Vv8SeQZkIld8C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd6c9049-62e8-41eb-9973-368d56c6841c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=11f0558c&sv=2)

# Permission Sets | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#overview)

**Overview**

A permission set is a group of permissions, divided in sections, that grants a set of rights and access to a user. The following default permission sets are included with ePO, for immediate assignment or for use as a template for customization:

*   **Executive Reviewer**: Provides view permissions to dashboards, events, contacts, and can view information that relates to the entire System Tree
    
*   **Global Reviewer**: Provides view access globally across functionality, products, and the System Tree, except for extensions, multi-server roll-up data, registered servers, and software
    
*   **Group Admin**: Provides view and change permissions across ePO features. Users, who are assigned this permission set, each need at least one more permission set that grants access to needed products and groups of the System Tree.
    
*   **Group Reviewer**: Provides view permissions across ePO features. Users, who are assigned this permission set, each need at least one more permission set that grants access to needed products and groups of the System Tree.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FXz0p3cfE1UhMAEKa_6hWSLGG1xpEQIRZz.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76823322&sv=2)

**The administrator can assign permission sets while creating a user account, when editing an existing user account, and when creating a new permission set. Administrators have permissions to all products and features and can create, edit, or delete permission sets. Users who are not administrators can do only those things permitted by their assigned permission sets.**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#default-permission-sets)

**Default Permission Sets**

Each permission set grants a set of rights and access to any user to which the permission set is assigned. Remember, administrators always have the rights and access do everything in ePO. As a best practice, use these default permission sets as templates to create new ones that meet your needs.

![* Note: Users need to be assigned to at least one set, granting them permissions to desired products and groups.](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FV9HQyTGPP4nlnYmr_bKFAxX8-jcP1teTw.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abdb0ea1&sv=2)

\* **Note**: Users need to be assigned to at least one set, granting them permissions to desired products and groups.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#configuration-guidelines)

**Configuration Guidelines**

*   Some permissions are exclusive to administrator.
    
*   Multiple permission sets aggregate combined rights and privileges.
    
*   Use default permission sets as templates.
    
*   You can map to Active Directory users using Active Directory groups.
    
*   Consider groups to support different access control levels.
    
*   New extensions may add new sections that require configuration for access.
    
*   Consider which products require users to have data access for queries.
    
*   For quick migration, export defined permission sets and import them to other ePO servers.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#duplicating-adding-or-deleting-permission-sets)

**Duplicating, Adding, or Deleting Permission Sets**

To duplicate, add, or delete a permission set, complete these steps:

1.  Select **Menu** \> **User Management** > **Permission Sets** to open the Permission Sets page.
    
2.  Take one of these actions:
    
    *   **Duplicate**: Select (highlight) the source and then select **Actions** > **Duplicate**.
        
    *   **Delete**: Select (highlight) the source and then select **Actions** > **Delete**.
        
    *   **New**: Click **New Permission Set** button.
        
    
3.  If duplicating or adding, type a meaningful name in the Name box, then click **OK** (if duplicate) or **Save** (if new).
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FGHuCEK5Y2qhPCUbR_fc1xa9C0ckOGE6KQ.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1452a94&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#authentication-types)

**Authentication Types**

Each authentication type has different configuration requirements.

*   **ePO Authentication**: ePO authentication uses the ePO account’s credentials. This is the default authentication method. You must enter and confirm a password.
    
*   **Windows Authentication**: If you use Windows authentication, enter the user’s Windows NT domain credentials. You can specify whether users authenticate:
    
    *   Against the domain that your ePO server is joined to and any other domains that have a trust relationship (default)
        
    *   Against a list of one or more domain controllers for domains that do not have a trust relationship
        
    *   Using a Windows Internet Name Service (WINS) server to look up the appropriate domain controller **Note**: If you have domain controllers or a WINS server, you must configure the Windows authentication server setting.
        
    
*   **Certificate-based Authentication**: For certificate-based authentication, upload certificate file. This automatically adds the personal certificate subject Distinguished Name (DN). The ePO server must be configured to allow certificate-based authentication.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#permissions-exclusive-to-administrator)

**Permissions Exclusive to Administrator**

The following are permissions exclusive to the administrator:

*   Create, edit, or delete source and fallback repositories
    
*   Change server settings
    
*   Add and delete user accounts
    
*   Add, delete and assign permission sets Import events into ePO databases and limit events stored there
    

**Administrators have all permissions to all products and features.**

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#card-title-2)

Editing Permission Sets

After duplicating or adding a new permission set, you can edit selected sections, as required.

![82MJPK4WOwp_8I_2-Edit%2520Permission%2520Sets_1.png](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F50gruWp9CA2eYzlB_zXYx5CQ5z2tQjI88.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59f3d8a6&sv=2)

In the left pane, make sure the duplicated or new permission set is selected (highlighted).

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F2uBw_MlfRwcS65NJ_9-En8LrkUz8EbqvU.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c1ac0ee&sv=2)

Click the **Edit** link for a specific section. Example: **System Tree access**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FnOVbWW2BXzkLQgMJ_O8szn3F3g2jth8-c.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8e8b8a0&sv=2)

Modify the permissions, as required, then click **Save**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F0X2_2mzPbJi0IeGe_pTU5grFTqjh24gPn.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4301ebce&sv=2)

Verify your changes display on the **Permission Sets** page.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets#exporting-all-or-importing)

**Exporting All or Importing**

You can also export and import permission sets.

*   To export all permission sets into an XML file, click **Export All**.
    
*   To import permission sets from an XML file exported from this or another ePO server, click **Import**.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FZ00osTFgMfWiVyY4_hjD1cRk4eikRdeYd.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73850e6e&sv=2)

# Contacts | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/contacts#overview)

**Overview**

Contacts are primarily used as a selection option when creating automatic responses in ePO.

Options available for Contacts include:

*   Creating a new contact
    
*   Edit existing contact
    
*   Delete an existing contact
    

![Menu &gt; User Management &gt; Contacts](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FDbvTJgDUTwFrUhSH_EgNzwA-vCtWiYih6.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a4da14f&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**User Management**_ > _**Contacts**_

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/contacts#contacts-in-automatic-responses)

**Contacts in Automatic Responses**

When creating and configuring an Automatic response in ePO, do the following to utilize the Contacts entries.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FAQAtRTI76RUxkLWW_yH1iS9bM6IlQVU_O.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1775220&sv=2)

1.  Create/edit the Automatic Response.
    
2.  Click the **Actions** tab and select **Send Email** as the action to be performed.
    
3.  Click the ellipsis next to **Recipients** and select the desired contact(s) entry.
    
4.  Click **OK**.
    
5.  Continue entering the automatic response information and click **Save**.
    

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/contacts#creating-a-new-contact)

**Creating a New Contact**

To create a new contact in ePO:

1.  Click **Menu** \> **User Management** > **Contacts**.
    
2.  Click **New Contact**.
    
3.  Enter in the first name of the contact in the **First name** field.
    
4.  Enter in the last name of the contact in the **Last name** field.
    
5.  Enter the contact email address in the **Email address** field.
    
6.  Click **Save**.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fv97BCkkU1-7wTKes_fct1OryDNuDegqub.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7a8dfa8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/contacts#editing-and-deleting-contacts)

**Editing and Deleting Contacts**

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FkV8ekZkFogD_hku6PzTOAw%2F1694489439%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DTW9uIFNlcCAxMSAxNTozMDozOSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FgkoLfWB4VT_4QhdS_aPBTrOzJxLPtvLgj.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a954c070&sv=2)

To edit or delete an existing contact in ePO:

1.  Click **Menu** \> **User Management** > **Contacts**.
    
2.  Select the contact you want to edit or delete.
    
3.  Click **Actions** \> **Edit** or **Delete**.
    
4.  Enter the desired changes into the appropriate field(s) (if editing).
    
5.  Click **Save**.
    

[PreviousPermission Sets](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/user-management/permission-sets)

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/disaster-recovery/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   Plan a disaster recovery strategy.
    
*   If using a separate restore sever, its configuration should closely mirror your primary ePO server hardware.
    
*   Regularly take a Disaster Recovery Snapshot.
    
*   Regularly perform backup and copy backup file, storing them in a safe and secure location.
    
*   During an ePO software recovery installation, you must supply the Disaster Recovery Keystore encryption passphrase.
    
*   Remember, registered executable files are not backed up. You must replace those executable files when you restore the ePO server.
    

In the next lesson, you will learn some basic techniques for troubleshooting ePO.

[PreviousRunning a Disaster Recovery Snapshot Simulation](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/disaster-recovery/running-a-disaster-recovery-snapshot-simulation)
[NextModule Intro](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/troubleshootings-basics/module-intro)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   The Dashboards page displays monitors to help you manage, monitor, and act on the health of ePO-managed systems.
    
*   A monitor can be anything from a chart‑based query to a small web application.
    
*   ePO provides default dashboards for a quick start, but also lets you create custom dashboard to meet your own needs.
    
*   As you install additional extensions or products, additional dashboards are added to the list.
    
*   ePO ships with its own querying and reporting capabilities, which are highly customizable, flexible, and easy to use.
    
*   Reports combine queries and other elements into PDF documents, enabling focused, offline analysis.
    
*   Queries are essentially questions you ask ePO, and answers are returned in various forms of charts and tables.
    
*   ePO provides an easy, four-step wizard, called the Query Builder, that you use to create and edit custom queries.
    
*   Groups and permission sets control access to queries and reports.
    

In the next lesson, you will learn how to use Disaster Recovery.

[PreviousBuilding a Report Simulation](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/building-a-report-simulation)
[NextModule Intro](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/disaster-recovery/module-intro)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

There are two basic ways to prepare your ePO environment for disaster recovery:

*   Disaster Recovery Snapshot Server task along with backup of the ePO database.
    
*   Manually using detailed steps identified in [KB66616(opens in a new tab)](https://kcm.trellix.com/corporate/index?page=content&id=KB66616)
    .
    

You can use the information in this lesson to help prepare and restore your ePO server back to a previous setting in the event of a disaster in your environment.

In this module, you will learn about how to prepare your ePO server for automated and manual disaster recovery.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/disaster-recovery/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Describe the Disaster Recovery feature and how it works
    
*   Explain how to use a server task to take a regular Snapshot
    
*   Take a Snapshot from the Dashboard

# Module Intro | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

There are three basic types of logging files available to help troubleshoot ePO errors:

*   Agent
    
*   Installation
    
*   Server
    

You can use the information in this lesson to help troubleshoot various types of ePO issues in your environment. In addition, you will learn about tools available for ePO troubleshooting.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/troubleshootings-basics/module-intro#module-objectives)

**Module Objectives**

By the end of this module, you should be able to:

*   Identify the three key logging types in ePO
    
*   Identify the main types of issues associated with the three main logging types
    
*   Troubleshoot basic issues by reviewing the identified log files for the associated issue
    
*   Identify the main tools used to troubleshoot ePO issues
    
*   Perform basic troubleshooting steps using these main tools
    

[PreviousModule Summary](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/disaster-recovery/module-summary)

# Creating a New Dashboard Simulation | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

Welcome to the Creating a New Dashboard simulation.

In this simulation, you will create a new private product monitoring dashboard and monitors to the newly created dashboard.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fop98wHKvYK4jZ55oAhXD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c632c18-fc56-4c27-a394-0f2d2c980c93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55c57a2c&sv=2)

# Reports | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#reports)

**Reports**

Generate reports to share information about your network environment with security administrators and other stakeholders. Reports are configurable documents that display data from one or more queries, drawing data from one or more databases. The most recently run result for every report is stored in the system and is readily available for viewing. You can restrict access to reports by using groups and permission sets in the same way you restrict access to queries. Reports and queries can use the same groups, and because reports primarily consist of queries, this configuration allows for consistent access control.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#reports-page)

**Reports Page**

The Reports page specifies the actions you can perform on the selected reports.

_**Click on the information (i) icons for detailed information.**_

![Reports Page.png](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FyTfrVhuIHNPnmO1M_6WAEXxYYPciN3p7R.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e95d38f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#create-new-report-from-selection)

**Create New Report from Selection**

From the Query page, you can launch the Report Layout with the details of a selected query.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FzmTUrf1TzIYEUuA8_Q5rwancIzs3x_LjK.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c57cced8&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#report-structure)

**Report Structure**

Reports contain several elements held within a basic format. While reports are highly customizable, they have a basic structure that contains all the varying elements.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FyD2_XInReXic6UFo_fW4xhpIqHxSkFIWR.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77015282&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#page-elements)

**Page Elements**

Page elements provide the content of the report. They can be combined in any order and may be duplicated as needed.

*   Elements that ePO provides:
    
    *   Images
        
    *   Page breaks
        
    *   Query Charts
        
    *   Text
        
    *   Query Tables
        
    
*   Dragged and dropped into report layout, then positioned
    
*   Can be combined in any order
    
*   Can be duplicated as needed
    

![Page elements.png](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FfOC5bHi6Bx5N5Hr9_zvPXxCB-ZaTt51R6.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3a284e3&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/dashboerds-queries-reports/reports#header-and-footer)

**Header and Footer**

There are six fixed locations within the header and footer that can contain different data fields: three are in the header, three in the footer.

The header contains a left-aligned logo and two right-aligned fields, one above the other. These fields can contain one of four values:

*   Nothing
    
*   Date/Time
    
*   Page Number
    
*   User name of the user running the report
    

The footer contains three fields. One left-aligned, one centered, and one right-aligned. These three fields contain the same values listed above, as well as custom text.

![By default, reports use the system setting for headers and footers. If you do not want this, deselect Use Default Server Setting.](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fol9Rxtquv3lV0Nuh_uyxJ7A3yhc1wwmhG.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7319459&sv=2)

By default, reports use the system setting for headers and footers. If you do not want this, deselect **Use Default Server Setting**.

To change the system settings for headers and footers, click **Menu** > **Configuration** \> **Server Settings**, then select **Printing and Exporting** and click **Edit**.

![Setting the Printing and Exporting settings in Server Settings will change the header/footer information globally for ePO. The settings for print and export are:Headers and footers for exported documents: Specifies the information and logo displayed on the headers and footers of the PDF or html reportEdit Logo: Takes you to the Edit Logo page, where you configure the logo used in the PDF or html with the exported dataDefault page size: Specifies the size of paper on which the PDF reports are printedDefault page orientation: Specifies whether information is displayed and printed as portrait or landscapeDirectory for scheduled exports: Specifies the location in the file system to which the file is saved](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FBJCcOR8wY3fskT_nF8zFfg%2F1694632483%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DV2VkIFNlcCAxMyAwNzoxNDo0MyBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FnTArClKV_hy7D7vo_jI0KSqFq86epjyNd.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0878f2c&sv=2)

Setting the Printing and Exporting settings in Server Settings will change the header/footer information globally for ePO. The settings for print and export are:

Setting the Printing and Exporting settings in Server Settings will change the header/footer information globally for ePO. The settings for print and export are:

*   **Headers and footers for exported documents**: Specifies the information and logo displayed on the headers and footers of the PDF or html report
    
*   **Edit Logo**: Takes you to the Edit Logo page, where you configure the logo used in the PDF or html with the exported data
    
*   **Default page siz**e: Specifies the size of paper on which the PDF reports are printed
    
*   **Default page orientation**: Specifies whether information is displayed and printed as portrait or landscape
    
*   **Directory for scheduled exports**: Specifies the location in the file system to which the file is saved

# Module Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/troubleshootings-basics/module-summary#key-points)

**Key Points**

*   There are three main logging types in ePO – Agent, Installer, Server.
    
*   Each of these logging types provide helpful details to assist in troubleshooting issues, such as agent connectivity, policy enforcement, installation & upgrade, Event Parser, and SQL issues.
    
*   There are various “free” external tools that can assist in troubleshooting basic ePO issues.

# Course Summary | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/summary/course-summary#key-takeaways)

**Key Takeaways**

ePO is a key component of the Security Management framework, providing unified management of endpoint, network, and data security products.

The Trellix Agent is the client-side component of ePO. You must install it on each system in your network that you want ePO to manage.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/summary/course-summary#key-features)

**Key Features**

*   **Flexible automation**
    
*   **Unified view of security**
    
*   **Simplified security operations**
    
*   **Integration**

# Client Task Management | Trellix ePolicy Orchestrator - On-prem 5.1

**Client Task Overview**

Client tasks automate system management activities, such as product deployment, upgrades, and updates.

1.  **Client Task Catalog**
    
    Applies the concept of logical objects to ePO client tasks. You can create client task objects for a variety of purposes without the need to assign them immediately. You can treat these objects as reusable components, when assigning and scheduling client tasks.
    
2.  **Client Tasks**
    
    Can be assigned at any level in the System Tree and are inherited by groups and systems lower in the tree. As with policies and policy assignments, you can break the inheritance for an assigned client task.
    
3.  **Client Task Objects**
    
    Can be shared across multiple registered ePO servers in your environment. When client task objects are set to be shared, each registered server receives a copy after your Share Client Task server task runs. Any changes made to the task are updated each time it runs. When a client task object is shared, only the owner of the object can modify its settings. An administrator, on the target server that receives a shared task, is not the owner for that shared task. None of the users on the target server is the owner for any shared task objects that the target receives. If modifications are necessary, the administrator can duplicate the task, and then make modifications on the duplicated task.
    

You can export and import client tasks for use with other ePO servers.

**Note**: The product extensions installed on ePO server determine which client tasks are available for a specific application.

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#client-tasks)

**Client Tasks**

![Menu &gt; Client Tasks](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fn6a40KbCJgNjhQr4_0LgfF6UJ7ILiraZz.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d912110a&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Client Tasks**_

*   **Client Task Catalog**: View and create client tasks
    
*   **Client Task Assignments**: Assign and manage client tasks from the System Tree group/subgroup levels
    
*   **Client Task Comparison**: Compare client tasks with similar characteristics
    

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#client-task-catalog)

**Client Task Catalog**

Use the Client Task Catalog to add and manage client tasks. A client task must be enabled and assigned to your managed systems to be available to be used in the ePO environment.

Some commonly used client tasks for Trellix Agent include:

*   **Trellix Agent Statistics**: Collects network bandwidth saved by the RelayServer, Peer to Peer, and SuperAgent hierarchical features
    
*   **Trellix Agent Wakeup**: Triggers an immediate Agent-Server Communication; this applies to Windows operating systems only
    
*   **Mirror Repositories**: Specifies a location on the managed system to replicate contents from the repository; this applies to Windows operating systems only
    
*   **Product Deployment**: Install a product on managed systems
    
*   **Product Update**: Update a product on managed systems
    

![Menu &gt; Client Task Catalog](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FjRS3N7EXH-cjtx0l_oP-XZXNNkHrRhX2Q.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=453b6c1b&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Client Task Catalog**_

As additional products are checked into ePO, client tasks for those products will be added. **Example**: Endpoint Security Threat Prevention will add the On-Demand Scans and Restore from Quarantine client tasks.

#### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#client-task-assignments)

**Client Task Assignments**

From the Client Task Assignments page, you can view and manage client task assignments. You can also get to this page from the **System Tree** > **Assigned Client Tasks** tab.

![Menu &gt; Client Task Assignments or System Tree &gt; Assigned Client Tasks tab](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2Fa6Xks6vzDD6P6SEt_5n_-HttN63yI-Kxv.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=def5c3ea&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Client Task Assignments**_ or _**System Tree**_ \> _**Assigned Client Tasks**_ tab

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#client-task-comparison)

**Client Task Comparison**

The Client Task Comparison tool is used to compare client tasks that are similar. This allows you to determine which settings are different and which are the same.

![Menu &gt; Client Tasks &gt; Client Task Comparison](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FWjUW0_9aIKCMKSoR_k3CyxVItdGF5lfEf.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc4c6c0a&sv=2)

_**Menu**_ \> _**Client Tasks**_ > _**Client Task Comparison**_

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#client-task-approvals)

**Client Task Approvals**

With ePO - On-prem, the administrator has the option to require an approval process before a new or updated client task is pushed out, reducing the risk of an error and assuring quality control.

As an administrator you can create permission sets for different policy user levels. You can choose client task management users need approval to make task changes The Permission Sets allow some client task users not only to create and modify client tasks, but also to approve or reject client tasks created by other users. To manage client task creation, you can create permission sets for users who can create and modify specific client tasks. For example, you can create permission sets that allow one user to change tasks and another user permission to approve or reject those changes.

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#card-title-21)
> 
> Client Task Approvals: Server Settings
> 
> As an administrator, you can lock down creation access for client tasks by configuring user accounts to require approval first when attempting to create client tasks.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F3VZM5bK0YXdTVEpDrJPo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc505e6f-13e1-4328-9395-454c302c488f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bab6c90b&sv=2)

Select **Menu** \> **Configuration** \> **Server Settings**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FRee5nCfHv5X0sPQCsniV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8f2e4af-f619-44f5-832e-bbf870645a7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=780b1287&sv=2)

Navigate to and select **Approvals** under the Setting Categories column and click **Edit**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FqNINKwwSZlpgALRLhCCx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58394146-1c69-46fb-a709-45aa906cbce0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f50212e&sv=2)

Select the _Users need approval for client task changes_ option and click **Save**.

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#card-title-25)
> 
> Summary
> 
> The client task approval step is now completed. Next, we need to create a permission set that forces user accounts to have an administrator review the client task creation.

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#card-title-27)
> 
> Client Task Approvals: Permission Sets
> 
> Now you can create and assign the newly created permission set rules for the user account.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252F5gtSQTO0YDa147a8meaJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d2952fa-e0b1-4da9-b5f4-1030810f6788&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39dc4a5c&sv=2)

Select **Menu** \> **User Management** > **Permission Sets**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fe974g5VBIIfv2I5wFdCV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc654c2ed-1fd9-4645-8586-cf9dc5502a83&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d751ee3&sv=2)

Click **New Permission Set** to create a new default entry. For this example, we are creating the permission set named _Client Task Approver_.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FpoOKuXxJ4AOa9Lz7eGTx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db925e7f9-cfc2-4225-89f5-9303addb5e39&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c43f14b2&sv=2)

On the Permissions Set page, navigate to **Client Task Management** and click **Edit**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252Fpl78dGYInrWLAk7ze0C0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fdc4c49-c7e3-4d3a-8081-c2f5d30136c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d38f527c&sv=2)

Select the _No Permission – Users cannot approve or decline task change requests_ option and click **Save**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FmMNtoeut8FNjeK2I9eQI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77cbcb62-500e-4885-833e-45925477f7e4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1de40f36&sv=2)

Navigate to a product entry in the list and click **Edit**. For this example, we will use **Trellix Agent**.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3241386954-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjmsGhOHPrgQSX87jFLLt%252Fuploads%252FiHDDsFWCMGQI5hwvAN7P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9acaa95a-653c-4e11-ad07-ac80cae3c404&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=120c1e28&sv=2)

Select the _**View and change settings**_ option for the _Trellix Agent: Tasks_ entry and click **Save**.

> ### 
> 
> [](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#card-title-34)
> 
> Summary
> 
> Once you have created the permission set, you can edit it to either assign it to an existing user or create a new user and assign it to that user.

* * *

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#sharing-client-task-objects)

**Sharing Client Task Objects**

Client task objects can be shared across multiple registered ePO servers in your environment. When client task objects are set to be shared, each registered server receives a copy after your Share Client Tasks server task runs. Any changes made to the task are updated each time it runs.

When a client task object is shared, only the owner of the object can modify its settings. Administrators on the target server that receives a shared task are not owners for that shared task. None of the users on the target server are owners for any shared task objects the target receives.

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2F9bNknPy3qLEsMk-C_WiCKHpVGFBsOmHeq.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8a58f4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#deleting-client-tasks)

**Deleting Client Tasks**

To delete client tasks:

1.  In the left pane of the Client Tasks Catalog, select a **Client Task Type**. **Example**: **McAfee (Trellix) Agent** > **Product Update**.
    
2.  In the right pane, select a client task.
    
3.  Click the **Delete** link for the selected task.
    
4.  When prompted, ensure you understand how this will affect other systems and click **OK**. **Note**: This also removes the task from where it was assigned in the System Tree.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FqEXsWthipla7o0Ps_QUYXnUt_e3rFQaFu.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77d3322e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/product-management/client-task-management#managing-client-tasks-from-the-system-tree)

**Managing Client Tasks from the System Tree**

You can also manage client tasks from the System Tree.

From the **Assigned Client Tasks** tab, you can:

*   **Reset Inheritance**: The Broken Inheritance shows which systems or groups do not inherit task. From this column, you can also reset the inheritance for a specific System Tree object. To do this, click the blue hyperlink from the **Broken Inheritance** column, select an entry in the **Node Name** column, then click **Reset Inheritance**.
    
*   **Edit Assignment**: Click the **Edit Assignment** link to launch Client Task Assignment Builder within the Client Task Catalog.
    
*   **New Client Task Assignment**: Select **Actions** \> **Edit Assignment** to launch Client Task Assignment Builder within the Client Task Catalog or click the default link to the right of the **Actions** drop-down.
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FuZ9ldOTG-1Xf_ihO_aMPBLtPxAaMEXLje.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=22c52d47&sv=2)

From the **Systems** tab, you can:

*   **Modify Tasks on a Single System**: Edit tasks for selected system
    
*   **Run Client Task Now**: Run a client task for a selected system
    

![](https://sirogy.gitbook.io/trellix-epolicy-orchestrator-on-prem-5.1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftraining.trellix.com%2Fcontent%2Felearningngx%2FAhnSgBAy7j7hIT_7H3aY2w%2F1693969305%2F0088YmZiUEJFNUlneVVCNnVIVG9rc3ZsOUtjbnk2Yk5iN1AvYUNTQWlxV0NxUVIvbzFnKzYwdnFDczFXSmY3TEk0Rw%3D%3DVHVlIFNlcCAwNSAxNTowMTo0NSBFRFQgMjAyMw%3D%3D%2Feot%2Fscormcontent%2Fassets%2FaVlCVqSGFYZ4QtK0_hcTQhjjYR8CHB8d0.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=883a022d&sv=2)
